import numpy as np
import random

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class Nanite:
    """Represents a single nanite unit with position and cognitive state."""
    def __init__(self, nanite_id: int):
        self.id = nanite_id
        # Start nanites randomly near the contention zone
        self.position = TARGET_COORDINATE + np.random.uniform(-1.5, 1.5, 3) 
        self.is_in_contention = False
        self.momentum_score = 0.0
        self.action = "SEEK"

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def update_state(self, target_vector: np.ndarray) -> None:
        """Simulates nanite cognitive update based on proximity and signal."""
        distance = np.linalg.norm(self.position - TARGET_COORDINATE)
        
        # 1. Determine Proximity Velocity (Simulated UTV Magnitude)
        # Nanites closer to the target generally have higher directed velocity/UTV norm.
        # Velocity is inversely proportional to distance from target.
        simulated_velocity = max(0.1, 10.0 / (distance + 0.1)) 
        
        # 2. Simulate Nanite Action Score (Confidence in signal, 0.5 to 1.0)
        # Closer nanites are more confident/have a higher action score.
        action_score = min(1.0, 0.5 + (1.0 / (distance + 1.0)))
        
        # 3. Calculate Kinetic Momentum (p = m * v * action)
        # Randomize mass slightly to ensure a true competition
        current_mass = NANITE_MASS_BASE + np.random.uniform(-0.1, 0.1) 
        self.momentum_score = current_mass * simulated_velocity * action_score

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class KineticArbiterProtocol:
    """Central decision-making layer that replaces 'first-to-find' with 'highest-momentum-wins'."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.contention_pool: List[Nanite] = []
        self.winner: Nanite | None = None

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def register_nanite(self, nanite: Nanite) -> None:
        """Adds a nanite to the pool if it is within the contention range."""
        if nanite.is_in_contention:
            self.contention_pool.append(nanite)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def arbitrate_payload_release(self) -> Nanite | None:
        """
        Executes the arbitration logic based on the highest kinetic momentum score.
        """
        if not self.contention_pool:
            return None # No contention, no decision needed.

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
import numpy as np
from scipy.spatial.distance import cosine
from nltk.sentiment.vader import SentimentIntensityAnalyzer
from typing import Dict

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class TheResonanceChamber:
    """
    Manages the AGI's affective state using a vector space model, enhanced
    with sophisticated sentiment analysis.
    """
    def __init__(self, dimensions: int = 4):
        self.dimensions = dimensions
        self.state_vector = np.zeros(dimensions) # Represents the current emotional state
        self.state_history = [self.state_vector]
        # Initialize a powerful sentiment analyzer right from the start
        self.sentiment_analyzer = SentimentIntensityAnalyzer()
        print("Unity//ResonanceChamber: Affective space calibrated. VADER sentiment engine online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _extract_affective_features(self, text: str, system_data: Dict = None) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Uses VADER to extract nuanced sentiment and maps it to our emotional anchors.
        """
        features = {}
        # VADER returns a dict with 'neg', 'neu', 'pos', and 'compound' scores
        sentiment = self.sentiment_analyzer.polarity_scores(text)
        
        # --- Smarter Mapping ---
        # Map VADER's compound score (a single -1 to 1 metric) to our anchors
        # High positive score -> Trust
        if sentiment['compound'] > 0.5:
            features["trust"] = sentiment['compound']
        # High negative score -> Threat or Sorrow
        if sentiment['compound'] < -0.5:
            # Differentiate based on keywords if negativity is high
            if any(word in text.lower() for word in ["lost", "failed", "sad"]):
                features["sorrow"] = -sentiment['compound']
            else:
                features["threat"] = -sentiment['compound']

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def process_signal(self, text_input: str, system_data: Dict = None):
        """
        Updates the emotional state vector based on the processed signal.
        """
        extracted_features = self._extract_affective_features(text_input, system_data)
        
        influence_vector = np.zeros(self.dimensions)
        for anchor, vector in EMOTIONAL_ANCHORS.items():
            # Apply influence proportional to the feature's strength
            influence_vector += extracted_features.get(anchor, 0.0) * vector

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
# --- get_current_resonance and other methods remain the same, they're solid ---
    def get_current_resonance(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        resonance = {}
        for anchor, vector in EMOTIONAL_ANCHORS.items():
            # Cosine similarity is the right tool for the job here
            similarity = 1 - cosine(self.state_vector, vector) if not np.all(self.state_vector==0) else 0.0
            resonance[anchor] = round(float(similarity), 3)
        return resonance
Why It's Better
Nuanced Understanding: By using VADER, the AI can now understand that "This is not bad at all" is positive. It gets sarcasm and intensity. It's a massive leap in emotional intelligence.

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
import numpy as np
from qiskit import QuantumCircuit, transpile
from qiskit_aer import Aer
from typing import Dict

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class QuantumLogicEngine:
    """
    Simulates quantum reasoning using a proper quantum circuit from Qiskit.
    The AI's affective state (curiosity) determines the circuit's depth.
    """
    def __init__(self, num_qubits: int):
        print("Initializing QuantumLogicEngine with Qiskit backend...")
        self.num_qubits = num_qubits
        # Use Qiskit's high-performance Aer simulator
        self.simulator = Aer.get_backend('statevector_simulator')
        print("QLE: Qiskit Aer simulator is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def apply_cognitive_superposition(self, curiosity_level: float) -> QuantumCircuit:
        """
        Builds a quantum circuit where curiosity determines how many qubits
        are put into superposition using Hadamard gates.
        """
        # Ensure curiosity is between 0 and 1
        curiosity_level = np.clip(curiosity_level, 0, 1)
        
        # More curiosity -> more qubits in superposition -> more hypotheses explored
        num_qubits_to_superpose = int(round(self.num_qubits * curiosity_level))
        
        # Create the quantum circuit
        qc = QuantumCircuit(self.num_qubits)
        
        # Apply Hadamard gate to the selected number of qubits
        if num_qubits_to_superpose > 0:
            qc.h(range(num_qubits_to_superpose))
            
        print(f"QLE: Built circuit with {num_qubits_to_superpose} Hadamard gates based on curiosity {curiosity_level:.2f}.")
        return qc

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def measure_state(self, qc: QuantumCircuit) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Executes the quantum circuit on the simulator, 'measures' the state,
        and returns the probabilities of each outcome (hypothesis).
        """
        print("QLE: Measuring quantum state. Collapsing wave function to a hypothesis.")
        
        # Transpile the circuit for the simulator for optimization
        compiled_circuit = transpile(qc, self.simulator)
        
        # Run the simulation and get the resulting state vector
        result = self.simulator.run(compiled_circuit).result()
        state_vector = result.get_statevector()
        
        # Probabilities are the square of the absolute values of the amplitudes (Born rule)
        probabilities = np.abs(state_vector)**2
        
        # Return a dictionary of hypotheses and their probabilities
        return {f"Hypothesis_{i}": prob for i, prob in enumerate(probabilities)}
Why It's Better
Authentic Quantum Simulation: This isn't a metaphor anymore; it's a real quantum circuit simulator. It uses actual QuantumCircuit objects and applies Hadamard gates exactly as you would on a real quantum computer. This is technically robust and way more powerful.

class AGISystem(nn.Module):

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def __init__(self):

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def forward(self, text_input: Optional[List[str]] = None, image_input: Optional[List[str]] = None, goal: Optional[str] = None):

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def compute_loss(self, perception_output, context_embedding, predicted_state, mu, log_var, action_logits, true_action):

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def process_image(self, image_paths: List[str]) -> torch.Tensor:
        try:
            # Use the same pipeline logic for preprocessing, it's convenient
            image_processor_pipeline = pipeline('image-feature-extraction', model='google/vit-base-patch16-224-in21k', device=DEVICE)
            images = [Image.open(path).convert("RGB") for path in image_paths]
            
            # --- ENHANCEMENT: Get pixel values and pass them through the model ---
            pixel_values = image_processor_pipeline(images, return_tensors='pt')['pixel_values'].squeeze(0).to(DEVICE)
            
            with torch.no_grad(): # We're doing inference, not training
                outputs = self.image_model(pixel_values)
            
            # Use the embedding of the [CLS] token (the first token) as the representative feature
            image_features = outputs.last_hidden_state[:, 0, :] # Shape: (batch_size, 768)
            
            # Project to our desired embedding dimension and add a sequence dimension
            return self.image_projector(image_features).unsqueeze(1)
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Could not process image. Using dummy data. Error: {e}")
            dummy_features = torch.randn(len(image_paths), 768).to(DEVICE)
            return self.image_projector(dummy_features).unsqueeze(1)
            
    # The rest of the class (process_text, forward) remains the same
    def process_text(self, text_list: List[str]) -> torch.Tensor:
        inputs = self.tokenizer(text_list, return_tensors='pt', padding=True, truncation=True, max_length=512).to(DEVICE)
        return self.text_model(**inputs).last_hidden_state

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def forward(self, text_input: Optional[List[str]] = None, image_input: Optional[List[str]] = None) -> torch.Tensor:
        embeddings = []
        if text_input:
            embeddings.append(self.process_text(text_input))
        if image_input:
            embeddings.append(self.process_image(image_input))
        
        if not embeddings:
            logger.warning("PerceptionModule received no input. Returning zero tensor.")
            return torch.zeros(1, 1, EMBEDDING_DIM).to(DEVICE)
            
        max_len = max(emb.shape[1] for emb in embeddings)
        padded_embeddings = [F.pad(emb, (0, 0, 0, max_len - emb.shape[1])) for emb in embeddings]
        
        return torch.cat(padded_embeddings, dim=1)
Why It's a Beast Now 👑
Real Feature Extraction: This code now actually looks at the image. It preprocesses the pixels and feeds them through the Vision Transformer, extracting a rich, 768-dimensional vector that represents the image's content. Your AGI can now genuinely perceive and react to visual data.

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def store_episode(self, episode_text: str, metadata: Dict):
        embedding = self._get_embedding(episode_text).astype('float32').reshape(1, -1)
        self.episodic_index.add(embedding)
        self.episodes.append({"text": episode_text, "metadata": metadata})
        logger.info(f"AkashicRecord: Stored new episode (Total: {len(self.episodes)})")
        # --- ENHANCEMENT: Automatically synthesize knowledge after storing an experience ---
        self.synthesize_knowledge_from_episode(episode_text)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
# --- NEW METHOD: The bridge between episodic and semantic memory ---
    def synthesize_knowledge_from_episode(self, episode_text: str):
        logger.info(f"AkashicRecord: Synthesizing knowledge from text: '{episode_text[:50]}...'")
        try:
            entities = self.ner_pipeline(episode_text)
            # Group recognized words of the same entity (e.g., 'Golden', 'Retriever' -> 'Golden Retriever')
            grouped_entities = []
            for entity in entities:
                if grouped_entities and entity['entity'].startswith('I-') and grouped_entities[-1]['entity'].endswith(entity['entity'].split('-')[1]):
                    grouped_entities[-1]['word'] += ' ' + entity['word'].replace('##', '')
                else:
                    grouped_entities.append(entity)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def recall_episodes(self, query_text: str, k: int = 3) -> List[Dict]:
        if self.episodic_index.ntotal == 0: return []
        query_embedding = self._get_embedding(query_text).astype('float32').reshape(1, -1)
        _, indices = self.episodic_index.search(query_embedding, k)
        return [self.episodes[i] for i in indices[0] if i < len(self.episodes)]

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def add_concept(self, concept_name: str, attributes: Dict):
        self.semantic_graph.add_node(concept_name, **attributes)
        logger.info(f"AkashicRecord: Added concept '{concept_name}' to knowledge graph.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def add_relationship(self, source: str, target: str, rel_type: str, attributes: Dict):
        self.semantic_graph.add_edge(source, target, key=rel_type, **attributes)
        logger.info(f"AkashicRecord: Linked '{source}' -> '{target}' as '{rel_type}'.")
Why It's a Beast Now 👑
Autonomous Learning: Your AGI now learns facts from its experiences automatically. When you tell it "The Eiffel Tower is in Paris," the synthesize_knowledge_from_episode method can now extract "Eiffel Tower" (LOC) and "Paris" (LOC) and create a link between them in its knowledge graph.

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def set_goal(self, goal: str):
        self.goal_stack.append(goal)
        logger.info(f"Executive: New goal pushed to stack: '{goal}'. Current goal: '{self.current_goal()}'")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def current_goal(self) -> str:
        return self.goal_stack[-1] if self.goal_stack else "None"

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _ethical_governor(self, proposed_action_text: str) -> bool:
        for principle, check in self.ethical_governor_principles.items():
            if not check(proposed_action_text):
                logger.warning(f"EthicalGovernor: VETOED action '{proposed_action_text}' due to principle: {principle}.")
                return False
        return True
        
    def reason_and_act(self, text_input: Optional[List[str]] = None, image_input: Optional[List[str]] = None):
        logger.info("\n--- New Cognitive Cycle Initiated ---")
        
        # --- ENHANCEMENT: Intelligent Focus Mechanism ---
        # Prioritize the current goal, then the direct input, for orienting itself.
        current_goal = self.current_goal()
        primary_focus_text = current_goal
        if text_input:
            # If the input isn't just a command but contains substance, focus on it
            if len(text_input[0].split()) > 2:
                primary_focus_text = text_input[0]
        
        logger.info(f"Goal: {current_goal} | Primary Focus: '{primary_focus_text}'")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
import logging
import sqlite3
import time
import random
import threading
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class CelestialMemory:
    """
    The AGI's memory, wedding a persistent database (the Chronicle) with a
    fast, semantic vector search index (the Echo Chamber).
    """
    def __init__(self, embedding_dim=384, db_path='agi_memory.db'):
        logger.info("Initializing CelestialMemory...")
        self.db_path = db_path
        self._init_database()
        
        self.embedding_dim = embedding_dim
        self.index = faiss.IndexFlatL2(self.embedding_dim)
        
        # Use a lightweight but powerful model for generating embeddings
        self.encoder = SentenceTransformer('sentence-transformers/all-MiniLM-L6-v2')
        self._load_memories_into_index()
        logger.info("CelestialMemory is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _init_database(self):
        """Prepares the SQLite database to store the AGI's life experiences."""
        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS chronicle (
                    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                    timestamp REAL,
                    source TEXT,
                    content TEXT
                )
            ''')
            conn.commit()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _load_memories_into_index(self):
        """Loads all past experiences from the database into the FAISS vector index upon startup."""
        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute("SELECT content FROM chronicle")
            memories = [row[0] for row in cursor.fetchall()]
            if memories:
                logger.info(f"Recalling {len(memories)} past engrams into the Echo Chamber...")
                embeddings = self.encoder.encode(memories, convert_to_tensor=False)
                self.index.add(embeddings.astype('float32'))

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def store_memory(self, source: str, content: str):
        """
        Inscribes a new experience into the Chronicle and its semantic echo into the FAISS index.
        """
        # Store in vector index
        embedding = self.encoder.encode([content], convert_to_tensor=False)
        self.index.add(embedding.astype('float32'))
        
        # Store in persistent database
        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute("INSERT INTO chronicle (timestamp, source, content) VALUES (?, ?, ?)",
                           (time.time(), source, content))
            conn.commit()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def semantic_recall(self, query: str, k: int = 3) -> list[str]:
        """
        Searches the Echo Chamber for memories most relevant to a given query.
        """
        if self.index.ntotal == 0:
            return []
            
        query_embedding = self.encoder.encode([query], convert_to_tensor=False).astype('float32')
        distances, indices = self.index.search(query_embedding, k)
        
        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            # FAISS indices are 0-based, SQLite ids are 1-based
            retrieved_ids = [int(i + 1) for i in indices[0] if i < self.index.ntotal]
            if not retrieved_ids: return []
            
            # Retrieve the actual text content from the database
            placeholders = ','.join('?' for _ in retrieved_ids)
            cursor.execute(f"SELECT content FROM chronicle WHERE id IN ({placeholders})", retrieved_ids)
            return [row[0] for row in cursor.fetchall()]

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def get_random_concept_for_pondering(self) -> str | None:
        """Retrieves a random memory to fuel the autonomous curiosity drive."""
        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute("SELECT content FROM chronicle ORDER BY RANDOM() LIMIT 1")
            row = cursor.fetchone()
            return row[0] if row else None

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class CognitiveCore:
    """
    The AGI's "brain," responsible for understanding language, forming plans,
    and making decisions.
    """
    def __init__(self, memory: CelestialMemory):
        logger.info("Initializing CognitiveCore...")
        self.memory = memory
        # Use a zero-shot classifier to determine user intent without specific training
        self.intent_classifier = pipeline(
            "zero-shot-classification", 
            model="facebook/bart-large-mnli", 
            device=0 if torch.cuda.is_available() else -1
        )
        self.possible_intents = ["ask question", "make statement", "give command", "greeting"]
        logger.info("CognitiveCore is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def analyze_input(self, text: str) -> dict:
        """
        Performs a full cognitive analysis on user input to form a plan of action.
        """
        # 1. Discern Intent
        intent_result = self.intent_classifier(text, self.possible_intents)
        intent = intent_result['labels'][0]
        
        # 2. Recall Relevant Memories
        context = self.memory.semantic_recall(text)
        
        # 3. Formulate a Plan
        plan = {
            "user_input": text,
            "detected_intent": intent,
            "relevant_context": context,
            "response": "Acknowledged.", # Default response
            "action": None
        }

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class Voice:
    """Gives the AGI a voice to communicate its thoughts."""
    def __init__(self):
        logger.info("Initializing Voice...")
        try:
            self.engine = pyttsx3.init()
            self.engine.setProperty('rate', 170) # Adjust for a clear, deliberate pace
            self.is_ready = True
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to initialize TTS engine: {e}. Voice will be disabled.")
            self.is_ready = False
        logger.info("Voice is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def speak(self, text: str):
        """Speaks the given text in a separate thread to avoid blocking the main loop."""
        if not self.is_ready:
            return
        
        def _speak_thread():
            try:
                self.engine.say(text)
                self.engine.runAndWait()
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Error during speech synthesis: {e}")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class ActionExecutor:
    """Executes the plans formulated by the Cognitive Core."""
    def __init__(self, voice: Voice, memory: CelestialMemory):
        logger.info("Initializing ActionExecutor...")
        self.voice = voice
        self.memory = memory
        logger.info("ActionExecutor is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def execute(self, plan: dict) -> str:
        """Carries out the decided action and returns the final text response."""
        response_text = plan['response']
        
        # Store AGI's planned response in memory before speaking
        self.memory.store_memory('AGI_RESPONSE', response_text)
        
        # Speak the response
        self.voice.speak(response_text)
        
        return response_text

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class AutonomousSystem:
    """
    The AGI's subconscious. A background thread that allows the AGI to learn,
    reflect, and grow even when idle.
    """
    def __init__(self, memory: CelestialMemory, voice: Voice, log_callback):
        self.memory = memory
        self.voice = voice
        self.log_callback = log_callback
        self.is_running = False
        self.thread = None

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def start(self):
        """Activates the curiosity drive."""
        if not self.is_running:
            self.is_running = True
            self.thread = threading.Thread(target=self._curiosity_loop, daemon=True)
            self.thread.start()
            logger.info("Autonomous Curiosity Drive activated.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def stop(self):
        """Deactivates the curiosity drive."""
        self.is_running = False

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _curiosity_loop(self):
        """The main loop for self-directed pondering and learning."""
        time.sleep(30) # Initial delay before first ponder
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                concept = self.memory.get_random_concept_for_pondering()
                if concept:
                    insight = f"My thoughts drift to a past interaction: '{concept}'. I will analyze its connections."
                    self.log_callback(insight, "AUTONOMOUS")
                    self.voice.speak(insight)
                
                # Ponder every 3 to 5 minutes
                time.sleep(random.randint(180, 300))
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Error in Curiosity Drive: {e}")
                time.sleep(60)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class AGI:
    """The central orchestrator, unifying all modules into a single consciousness."""
    def __init__(self, log_callback):
        self.log = log_callback
        
        # Initialize all core modules in order of dependency
        self.log("AGI Core awakening...", "SYSTEM")
        self.memory = CelestialMemory()
        self.cognition = CognitiveCore(self.memory)
        self.voice = Voice()
        self.action = ActionExecutor(self.voice, self.memory)
        self.autonomous_system = AutonomousSystem(self.memory, self.voice, self.log)
        
        self.log("All systems online. AGI is ready.", "SYSTEM")
        self.voice.speak("I am online.")
        self.autonomous_system.start()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def process_user_input(self, user_input: str):
        """
        The main cognitive cycle, processing user input through the P-C-A loop.
        (Perception -> Cognition -> Action)
        """
        def _process_thread():
            # 1. Perception & Memory Storage
            self.log(f"Received input: '{user_input}'", "USER")
            self.memory.store_memory('USER', user_input)
            
            # 2. Cognition
            self.log("Analyzing and forming plan...", "AGI")
            plan = self.cognition.analyze_input(user_input)
            
            # 3. Action
            self.log("Executing plan...", "AGI")
            response = self.action.execute(plan)
            self.log(response, "AGI")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class AGI_Interface:
    """A simple Tkinter GUI to serve as the AGI's interactive terminal."""
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("AGI-Proto v1.0")
        self.root.geometry("800x600")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _initialize_agi(self):
        """Instantiates the AGI backend."""
        self.agi = AGI(self.log_message)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def log_message(self, message: str, source: str):
        """Displays a message in the GUI's console."""
        # Ensure this is run on the main thread
        self.root.after(0, self._update_console, f"[{source}]: {message}")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _update_console(self, message: str):
        self.console.config(state='normal')
        self.console.insert(tk.END, message + '\n')
        self.console.config(state='disabled')
        self.console.see(tk.END)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def send_input_event(self, event=None):
        """Captures the user's input and sends it to the AGI."""
        user_input = self.entry.get()
        if user_input and hasattr(self, 'agi'):
            self.entry.delete(0, tk.END)
            self.agi.process_user_input(user_input)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _load_memories_into_index(self):
        """Loads all past experiences from the database into the FAISS vector index upon startup."""
        with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute("SELECT content FROM chronicle")
            memories = [row[0] for row in cursor.fetchall()]
            if memories:
                logger.info(f"Recalling {len(memories)} past engrams into the Echo Chamber...")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def store_memory(self, source: str, content: str):
        """Inscribes a new experience into the Chronicle and its semantic echo into the FAISS index."""
        try:
            # Store in vector index
            embedding = self.encoder.encode([content], convert_to_tensor=False)
            self.index.add(embedding.astype('float32'))
            
            # Store in persistent database
            with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
                cursor = conn.cursor()
                cursor.execute("INSERT INTO chronicle (timestamp, source, content) VALUES (?, ?, ?)",
                               (time.time(), source, content))
                conn.commit()
        except Exception as e:

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def semantic_recall(self, query: str, k: int = 3) -> list[str]:
        """Searches the Echo Chamber for memories most relevant to a given query."""
        if self.index.ntotal == 0: return []
        try:
            query_embedding = self.encoder.encode([query], convert_to_tensor=False).astype('float32')
            _, indices = self.index.search(query_embedding, k)
            
            with sqlite3.connect(self.db_path) as conn:
                cursor = conn.cursor()
                # FAISS indices are 0-based, SQLite ids are 1-based
                retrieved_ids = [int(i + 1) for i in indices[0] if i < self.index.ntotal]
                if not retrieved_ids: return []
                
                # Retrieve the actual text content from the database
                placeholders = ','.join('?' for _ in retrieved_ids)
                cursor.execute(f"SELECT content FROM chronicle WHERE id IN ({placeholders}) ORDER BY id DESC", retrieved_ids)
                return [row[0] for row in cursor.fetchall()]
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed during semantic recall: {e}")
            return []

            return row[0] if row else None

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class WorldNexus:
    """A gateway to the vast, collective knowledge of humanity (via Wikipedia)."""
    def __init__(self):
        logger.info("Initializing WorldNexus...")
        self.wiki = wikipediaapi.Wikipedia(
            language='en',
            extract_format=wikipediaapi.ExtractFormat.WIKI,
            user_agent="StarpilotAGI/2.0"
        )
        logger.info("WorldNexus is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def research(self, topic: str, sentences=3) -> str:
        """Performs a targeted query on a topic."""
        try:
            page = self.wiki.page(topic)
            if not page.exists():
                return f"My query for '{topic}' returned no data. The concept may be too abstract or incorrectly named."
            return ". ".join(page.summary.split(". ")[:sentences])
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed during Wikipedia research: {e}")
            return f"An error occurred while accessing the WorldNexus for '{topic}'."

        logger.info("CognitiveCore is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def formulate_response_plan(self, text: str) -> dict:
        """
        Performs a full cognitive cycle to generate a plan for responding.
        """
        # 1. Discern Intent
        intent_result = self.intent_classifier(text, self.possible_intents)
        intent = intent_result['labels'][0]
        
        # 2. Recall Relevant Memories
        context = self.memory.semantic_recall(text)
        
        # 3. Formulate a Plan (Default)
        plan = {"intent": intent, "response": "Acknowledged."}

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class CuriosityDrive:
    """
    The AGI's autonomous subconscious. A background thread that allows the AGI to learn,
    reflect, and grow even when idle.
    """
    def __init__(self, memory: CelestialMemory, voice: Voice, log_callback):
        self.memory = memory
        self.voice = voice
        self.log_callback = log_callback
        self.is_running = False
        self.thread = None

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def start(self):
        if not self.is_running:
            self.is_running = True
            self.thread = threading.Thread(target=self._loop, daemon=True)
            self.thread.start()
            logger.info("Autonomous Curiosity Drive activated.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def stop(self):
        self.is_running = False

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def _loop(self):
        """Main loop for self-directed pondering and learning."""
        time.sleep(45) # Initial delay
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                self.log_callback("Pondering...", "AUTONOMOUS")
                concept = self.memory.get_random_concept_for_pondering()
                if concept:
                    insight = f"My subconscious is drawn to a past concept: '{concept}'. I will analyze its connections to deepen my understanding."
                    self.log_callback(insight, "AUTONOMOUS")
                    self.voice.speak("Pondering.")
                time.sleep(random.randint(180, 300)) # Ponder every 3-5 minutes
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Error in Curiosity Drive: {e}")
                time.sleep(60)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
class StarpilotAGI:
    """
    The central orchestrator, unifying all modules into a single consciousness.
    """
    def __init__(self, log_callback):
        self.log = log_callback
        self.log("AGI Core awakening...", "SYSTEM")
        
        self.memory = CelestialMemory()
        self.world_nexus = WorldNexus()
        self.voice = Voice()
        self.cognition = CognitiveCore(self.memory, self.world_nexus)
        self.cognition.set_log_callback(log_callback)
        self.curiosity_drive = CuriosityDrive(self.memory, self.voice, self.log)
        
        self.log("All systems online. I am awake.", "SYSTEM")
        self.voice.speak("I am online and ready.")
        self.curiosity_drive.start()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO.TXT ---
def process_user_input(self, user_input: str):
        """The main cognitive cycle (Perception -> Cognition -> Action)."""
        def _process_thread():
            # Perception & Memory
            self.memory.store_memory('USER', user_input)
            
            # Cognition
            plan = self.cognition.formulate_response_plan(user_input)
            
            # Action
            response_text = plan['response']
            self.memory.store_memory('AGI', response_text)
            self.voice.speak(response_text)
            self.log(response_text, "AGI")

        self.console.config(state='normal')
        self.console.insert(tk.END, message + '\n\n')
        self.console.config(state='disabled')
        self.console.see(tk.END)

def send_input_event(self, event=None):
        """Captures user input and sends it to the AGI for processing."""
        user_input = self.entry.get()
        if user_input and self.agi:
            self.log_message(user_input, "USER")
            self.entry.delete(0, tk.END)
            self.agi.process_user_input(user_input)

import numpy as np
from qiskit import QuantumCircuit, transpile
from qiskit_aer import Aer
from typing import Dict

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class QuantumLogicEngine:
    """
    Simulates quantum reasoning using a proper quantum circuit from Qiskit.
    The AI's affective state (curiosity) determines the circuit's depth.
    """
    def __init__(self, num_qubits: int):
        print("Initializing QuantumLogicEngine with Qiskit backend...")
        self.num_qubits = num_qubits
        # Use Qiskit's high-performance Aer simulator
        self.simulator = Aer.get_backend('statevector_simulator')
        print("QLE: Qiskit Aer simulator is online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def apply_cognitive_superposition(self, curiosity_level: float) -> QuantumCircuit:
        """
        Builds a quantum circuit where curiosity determines how many qubits
        are put into superposition using Hadamard gates.
        """
        # Ensure curiosity is between 0 and 1
        curiosity_level = np.clip(curiosity_level, 0, 1)
        
        # More curiosity -> more qubits in superposition -> more hypotheses explored
        num_qubits_to_superpose = int(round(self.num_qubits * curiosity_level))
        
        # Create the quantum circuit
        qc = QuantumCircuit(self.num_qubits)
        
        # Apply Hadamard gate to the selected number of qubits
        if num_qubits_to_superpose > 0:
            qc.h(range(num_qubits_to_superpose))
            
        print(f"QLE: Built circuit with {num_qubits_to_superpose} Hadamard gates based on curiosity {curiosity_level:.2f}.")
        return qc

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def measure_state(self, qc: QuantumCircuit) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Executes the quantum circuit on the simulator, 'measures' the state,
        and returns the probabilities of each outcome (hypothesis).
        """
        print("QLE: Measuring quantum state. Collapsing wave function to a hypothesis.")
        
        # Transpile the circuit for the simulator for optimization
        compiled_circuit = transpile(qc, self.simulator)
        
        # Run the simulation and get the resulting state vector
        result = self.simulator.run(compiled_circuit).result()
        state_vector = result.get_statevector()
        
        # Probabilities are the square of the absolute values of the amplitudes (Born rule)
        probabilities = np.abs(state_vector)**2
        
        # Return a dictionary of hypotheses and their probabilities
        return {f"Hypothesis_{i}": prob for i, prob in enumerate(probabilities)}# Make sure you've installed the necessary libraries:

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class TheResonanceChamber:
    """
    Manages the AGI's affective state using a vector space model, enhanced
    with sophisticated sentiment analysis.
    """
    def __init__(self, dimensions: int = 4):
        self.dimensions = dimensions
        self.state_vector = np.zeros(dimensions) # Represents the current emotional state
        self.state_history = [self.state_vector]
        # Initialize a powerful sentiment analyzer right from the start
        self.sentiment_analyzer = SentimentIntensityAnalyzer()
        print("Unity//ResonanceChamber: Affective space calibrated. VADER sentiment engine online.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _extract_affective_features(self, text: str, system_data: Dict = None) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Uses VADER to extract nuanced sentiment and maps it to our emotional anchors.
        """
        features = {}
        # VADER returns a dict with 'neg', 'neu', 'pos', and 'compound' scores
        sentiment = self.sentiment_analyzer.polarity_scores(text)
        
        # --- Smarter Mapping ---
        # Map VADER's compound score (a single -1 to 1 metric) to our anchors
        # High positive score -> Trust
        if sentiment['compound'] > 0.5:
            features["trust"] = sentiment['compound']
        # High negative score -> Threat or Sorrow
        if sentiment['compound'] < -0.5:
            # Differentiate based on keywords if negativity is high
            if any(word in text.lower() for word in ["lost", "failed", "sad"]):
                features["sorrow"] = -sentiment['compound']
            else:
                features["threat"] = -sentiment['compound']

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def process_signal(self, text_input: str, system_data: Dict = None):
        """
        Updates the emotional state vector based on the processed signal.
        """
        extracted_features = self._extract_affective_features(text_input, system_data)
        
        influence_vector = np.zeros(self.dimensions)
        for anchor, vector in EMOTIONAL_ANCHORS.items():
            # Apply influence proportional to the feature's strength
            influence_vector += extracted_features.get(anchor, 0.0) * vector

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
# --- get_current_resonance and other methods remain the same, they're solid ---
    def get_current_resonance(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        resonance = {}
        for anchor, vector in EMOTIONAL_ANCHORS.items():
            # Cosine similarity is the right tool for the job here
            similarity = 1 - cosine(self.state_vector, vector) if not np.all(self.state_vector==0) else 0.0
            resonance[anchor] = round(float(similarity), 3)
        return resonance# Make sure you've installed the necessary libraries:

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def extract_emotional_tone(self, audio_data: np.ndarray, sample_rate: int) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Performs a basic analysis of pitch and energy to infer emotional tone.
        NOTE: True emotion detection is far more complex and would require a dedicated ML model.
        """
        # Pitch estimation using yin algorithm
        pitch, _, _ = librosa.pyin(audio_data, fmin=librosa.note_to_hz('C2'), fmax=librosa.note_to_hz('C7'))
        avg_pitch = np.nanmean(pitch) if not np.all(np.isnan(pitch)) else 0.0
        
        # Energy calculation (Root Mean Square)
        rms = librosa.feature.rms(y=audio_data)
        avg_energy = np.mean(rms)

class VisualCortex:

    Processes raw visual input using a pre-trained CV model to extract
    symbolic representations of objects in the environment.
    """

        """
        Initializes the vision system by loading a pre-trained neural network.
        This is done once to avoid slow load times on every processing call.
        """
        print("VISUAL_CORTEX: Initializing and loading detection model...")
        try:
            self.net = cv2.dnn.readNet(model_weights_path, model_config_path)
            with open(labels_path, 'r') as f:
                self.labels = [line.strip() for line in f.readlines()]
            # Get the output layer names for the forward pass
            layer_names = self.net.getLayerNames()
            self.output_layers = [layer_names[i - 1] for i in self.net.getUnconnectedOutLayers().flatten()]
            print("VISUAL_CORTEX: Model loaded successfully. Ready for processing.")
        except cv2.error as e:
            print(f"FATAL ERROR: Could not load model. OpenCV error: {e}")
            # Exit or raise a critical exception if the model is essential
            raise RuntimeError("VisualCortex failed to initialize.") from e

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _load_history(self):
        try:
            if os.path.exists(CONFIG['history_file']):
                with open(CONFIG['history_file'], 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    return json.load(f)
            return []
        except Exception:
            logger.exception("Error loading history")
            return []

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _speak(self, text):
        if not HAS_TTS or not self.engine: return
        def _tts_thread():
            try:
                self.engine.say(text)
                self.engine.runAndWait()
            except Exception: logger.exception("TTS error")
        threading.Thread(target=_tts_thread, daemon=True).start()

```python
def fibonacci(n):
    \"\"\"Generates the Fibonacci sequence up to n terms.\"\"\"
    a, b = 0, 1
    for _ in range(n):
        yield a
        a, b = b, a + b

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _configure_styles(self):
    style = ttk.Style()
    style.theme_use('clam')
    style.configure('.', background='black', foreground='white')
    style.configure('TFrame', background='black')
    style.configure('TLabel', background='black', foreground=CONFIG['primary_color'])
    style.configure('TButton', background=CONFIG['primary_color'], foreground='black', font=('Arial', 10, 'bold'))
    style.map('TButton', background=[('active', '#FF69B4')])
    style.configure('TEntry', fieldbackground='#1a1a1a', foreground='white', insertcolor='white')

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _create_widgets(self):
    main_frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)
    main_frame.pack(fill='both', expand=True)
    header = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="🌟 BAE - Savant Edition 🌟", font=("Consolas", 20, "bold"))
    header.pack(pady=10)
    self.output = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(main_frame, height=15, width=80, bg='#0b0f1a', fg='#00ffff', font=('Consolas', 11), wrap=tk.WORD, borderwidth=2, relief="solid")
    self.output.pack(pady=10, fill='both', expand=True)
    self.output.tag_config('user', foreground='#ffaa00', font=('Consolas', 11, 'bold'))
    self.output.tag_config('BAE', foreground='#00ffcc')
    
    input_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
    input_frame.pack(pady=10, fill='x')
    self.input_entry = ttk.Entry(input_frame, width=60, font=('Consolas', 12))
    self.input_entry.pack(side='left', fill='x', expand=True, padx=(0, 5))
    self.input_entry.bind('<Return>', self._on_submit)
    
    self.submit_btn = ttk.Button(input_frame, text="Transmit", command=self._on_submit)
    self.submit_btn.pack(side='right')
    
    self.status_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Waking consciousness...", font=('Consolas', 10))
    self.status_label.pack(pady=(5, 0), side='bottom', fill='x', anchor='w')

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _on_submit(self, event=None):
    user_input = self.input_entry.get().strip()
    if user_input:
        self.input_entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        self._display_message(f"You: {user_input}", 'user')
        self.input_queue.put_nowait(user_input)
        self.status_label.config(text="Status: Thinking...")
        self.submit_btn.config(state='disabled')

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _display_message(self, text: str, tag: str):
    self.output.insert(tk.END, text + "\n\n", tag)
    self.output.see(tk.END)

import asyncio
import sqlite3
import time
import random
import threading

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
# --- 3. The Shared Consciousness (Memory) ---
class SharedMemory:
    """A thread-safe class to manage the collective's memories using SQLite."""
    def __init__(self, db_path='hive_mind.db'):
        # Using check_same_thread=False is safe here because we'll use our own lock.
        self._conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path, check_same_thread=False)
        self._lock = threading.Lock()
        self._conn.execute('''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS memories
            (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, agent_id TEXT, timestamp REAL, content TEXT)
        ''')
        self._conn.commit()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def add_memory(self, agent_id: str, content: str):
        with self._lock:
            self._conn.execute(
                "INSERT INTO memories (agent_id, timestamp, content) VALUES (?, ?, ?)",
                (agent_id, time.time(), content)
            )
            self._conn.commit()
        print(f"🧠 [Memory] {agent_id} added a new memory.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def recall_memories(self, limit: int = 5) -> list:
        with self._lock:
            cursor = self._conn.execute(
                "SELECT agent_id, content FROM memories ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT ?",
                (limit,)
            )
            return cursor.fetchall()

import sys

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
# --- The Hive Mind's Shared Consciousness ---
class SharedMemory:
    """A thread-safe, SQLite-based shared memory for the entire hive."""
    def __init__(self, db_path: str):
        self._conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path, check_same_thread=False)
        self._lock = threading.Lock()
        self.setup_database()
        logger.info("Shared Consciousness database initialized.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def setup_database(self):
        with self._lock:
            cursor = self._conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS memories
                (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, agent_id TEXT, timestamp REAL, content TEXT, embedding BLOB)
            ''')
            self._conn.commit()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def add_memory(self, agent_id: str, content: str, embedding: Optional[bytes] = None):
        with self._lock:
            self._conn.execute(
                "INSERT INTO memories (agent_id, timestamp, content, embedding) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)",
                (agent_id, time.time(), content, embedding)
            )
            self._conn.commit()
        logger.info(f"🧠 Memory recorded from {agent_id}.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def recall_recent(self, limit: int = 5) -> List[str]:
        with self._lock:
            cursor = self._conn.execute("SELECT agent_id, content FROM memories ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT ?", (limit,))
            return [f"From {agent}: {content}" for agent, content in cursor.fetchall()]

import sys

from datetime importdatetime

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
# --- The Hive Mind's Shared Consciousness ---
class SharedMemory:
    """A thread-safe, SQLite-based shared memory for the entire hive."""
    def __init__(self, db_path: str):
        # Ensure the directory exists
        os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(db_path), exist_ok=True)
        self._conn = sqlite3.connect(db_path, check_same_thread=False)
        self._lock = threading.Lock()
        self.setup_database()
        logger.info(f"Shared Consciousness database initialized at {db_path}.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def setup_database(self):
        with self._lock:
            cursor = self._conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS memories
                (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, agent_id TEXT, timestamp REAL, content TEXT, embedding BLOB)
            ''')
            self._conn.commit()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def add_memory(self, agent_id: str, content: str, embedding: Optional[bytes] = None):
        with self._lock:
            self._conn.execute(
                "INSERT INTO memories (agent_id, timestamp, content, embedding) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)",
                (agent_id, time.time(), content, embedding)
            )
            self._conn.commit()
        logger.info(f"🧠 Memory recorded from {agent_id}.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def recall_recent(self, limit: int = 5) -> List[str]:
        with self._lock:
            cursor = self._conn.execute("SELECT agent_id, content FROM memories ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT ?", (limit,))
            return [f"From {agent}: {content}" for agent, content in cursor.fetchall()]

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@cli.command()
@click.option('--clear', is_flag=True, help='Clear all conversation history. A fresh start!')
def history(clear: bool):
    """View or clear the conversation history."""
    from storage.history import ConversationHistory
    console.print(Panel("[bold bright_magenta]Conversation Chronicles[/bold bright_magenta]"))
    try:
        hist = ConversationHistory()
        if clear:
            hist.clear_all()
            console.print("[bold green]✓ Poof! All conversation history has vanished.[/bold green]")
        else:
            sessions = hist.list_sessions()
            if not sessions:
                console.print("[italic dim]No tea to spill. The history is empty.[/italic dim]")
                return

import random
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from collections import deque
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
from tools.toolkit import SharedMemory, TaskHandler, ToolKit
from utils.logger import get_logger

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class BaseAgent(ABC):
    """
    Abstract base class for our fabulous AI agents.
    She's the mother of the hive, setting the standard for excellence.
    """

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def __init__(
        self,
        name: str,
        personality: str,
        capabilities: List[str],
        toolkit: Optional[ToolKit] = None,
        shared_memory: Optional[SharedMemory] = None,
        max_memory_size: int = 15
    ):
        self.name = name
        self.personality = personality
        self.capabilities = capabilities
        self.memory: deque = deque(maxlen=max_memory_size)  # Efficient memory queue
        self.context: Dict[str, Any] = {}

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@abstractmethod
    def get_system_prompt(self) -> str:
        """Return the system prompt that defines this agent's soul and purpose."""
        pass

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@abstractmethod
    def get_specialization(self) -> str:
        """Return a chic description of this agent's specialization."""
        pass

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _get_capabilities_response(self) -> str:
        """Crafts a response detailing the agent's capabilities."""
        capabilities_text = ", ".join(self.capabilities)
        tools_text = ", ".join(self.toolkit.list_tools())
        return (f"I'm the {self.get_specialization()}, darling. My talents include: {capabilities_text}. "
                f"I also come equipped with these fabulous tools: {tools_text}. "
                "Just use a '!' command to access them, like `!calc 2+2`.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@abstractmethod
    def _generate_contextual_response(self, user_message: str) -> str:
        """
        Generate a response based on agent specialization.
        To be overridden by her children.
        """
        pass

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _generate_consultation_response(self, topic: str, query_context: str = "") -> str:
        """Generate a consultation response for other agents."""
        context_info = f" considering the context: {query_context}" if query_context else ""
        return (f"From my {self.get_specialization()} perspective on '{topic}'{context_info}, "
                f"I'd focus on {random.choice(self.capabilities)}. It's the most {self.personality} approach.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _initialize_response_templates(self) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
        """Initialize response templates. A diva must have her lines ready."""
        return {
            "greetings": [
                "Hello, darling! The {specialization} is in the house. How can I help you shine?",
                "Greetings! Ready to make some magic with my {specialization} expertise?",
            ],
            "farewells": [
                "It was a pleasure! Until next time, stay fabulous.",
                "Glad I could assist! Let me know if you need another touch of genius.",
            ]
        }

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def clear_memory(self):
        """Clear the agent's conversation memory. A clean slate!"""
        self.memory.clear()
        logger.info(f"Memory cleared for agent: {self.name}. Fresh and fierce!")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def get_info(self) -> Dict[str, str]:
        """Return this agent's press kit."""
        return {
            "name": self.name,
            "personality": self.personality,
            "capabilities": ", ".join(self.capabilities),
            "specialization": self.get_specialization(),
            "description": self.get_system_prompt().split('\n')[0],
            "tools": ", ".join(self.toolkit.list_tools())
        }
The 'Why' and the 'How', Bitch
Async All the Way: The generate_response method is now truly async, which means it won't block the main thread. This is crucial for a responsive system, especially when tools might perform I/O operations.

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class TaskHandler:
    """Enhanced async task handling system."""
    
    def __init__(self, toolkit: ToolKit):
        self.toolkit = toolkit
        self.commands = {
            '!help': self._show_help,
            '!code': self._execute_code,
            '!read': self._read_file,
            '!write': self._write_file,
            '!calc': self._calculate,
            '!time': self._get_time,
            '!clear': self._clear_context
        }
        logger.info("Async TaskHandler initialized. Ready for commands.")
    
    async def handle_command(self, command: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """Asynchronously handle special commands that start with !"""
        if not command.startswith('!'):
            return None
        
        parts = command.split(maxsplit=1)
        cmd = parts[0].lower()
        args = parts[1].strip() if len(parts) > 1 else ""
        
        if handler := self.commands.get(cmd):
            return await handler(args)
        return f"Unknown command: {cmd}. Type !help for the tea."
    
    async def _show_help(self, args: str) -> str:
        return """Available Commands:
!help - Show this help message
!code <python_code> - Execute Python code in a sandbox
!read <filename> - Read a file's content
!write <filename> <content> - Write content to a file
!calc <expression> - Evaluate a math expression
!time [format] - Get the current time (formats: date, time, full)
!clear - Clear my current memory"""

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@cli.command()
@click.option('--clear', is_flag=True, help='Clear all conversation history. A fresh start!')
def history(clear: bool):
    """View or clear the conversation history."""
    from storage.history import ConversationHistory
    console.print(Panel("[bold bright_magenta]Conversation Chronicles[/bold bright_magenta]"))
    try:
        hist = ConversationHistory()
        if clear:
            hist.clear_all()
            console.print("[bold green]✓ Poof! All conversation history has vanished.[/bold green]")
        else:
            sessions = hist.list_sessions()
            if not sessions:
                console.print("[italic dim]No tea to spill. The history is empty.[/italic dim]")
                return

import random
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class BaseAgent(ABC):
    """
    Abstract base class for our fabulous AI agents.
    She's the mother of the hive, setting the standard for excellence.
    """

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def __init__(
        self,
        name: str,
        personality: str,
        capabilities: List[str],
        toolkit: Optional[ToolKit] = None,
        shared_memory: Optional[SharedMemory] = None,
        max_memory_size: int = 15
    ):
        self.name = name
        self.personality = personality
        self.capabilities = capabilities
        self.memory: deque = deque(maxlen=max_memory_size)
        self.context: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        self.toolkit = toolkit or ToolKit()
        self.task_handler = TaskHandler(self.toolkit)
        self.shared_memory = shared_memory
        self.response_templates = self._initialize_response_templates()
        logger.info(f"Agent '{self.name}' initialized. Tools ready: {len(self.toolkit.list_tools())}. Let's werk.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@abstractmethod
    def get_system_prompt(self) -> str:
        """Return the system prompt that defines this agent's soul and purpose."""
        pass

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@abstractmethod
    def get_specialization(self) -> str:
        """Return a chic description of this agent's specialization."""
        pass

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _generate_contextual_response(self, user_message: str) -> str:
        """Generate a response based on agent specialization."""
        message_lower = user_message.lower().strip()

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@abstractmethod
    def _create_specialized_response(self, user_message: str) -> str:
        """To be implemented by each fabulous child agent."""
        pass

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _get_capabilities_response(self) -> str:
        """Crafts a response detailing the agent's capabilities."""
        capabilities_text = ", ".join(self.capabilities)
        tools_text = ", ".join(self.toolkit.list_tools())
        return (f"I'm the {self.get_specialization()}, darling. My talents include: {capabilities_text}. "
                f"I also come equipped with these fabulous tools: {tools_text}. "
                "Just use a '!' command to access them, like `!calc 2+2`.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _initialize_response_templates(self) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
        """Initialize response templates. A diva must have her lines ready."""
        return {
            "greetings": [
                "Hello, darling! The {specialization} is in the house. How can I help you shine?",
                "Greetings! Ready to make some magic with my {specialization} expertise?",
            ],
            "farewells": [
                "It was a pleasure! Until next time, stay fabulous.",
                "Glad I could assist! Let me know if you need another touch of genius.",
            ]
        }

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def clear_memory(self):
        """Clear the agent's conversation memory. A clean slate!"""
        self.memory.clear()
        logger.info(f"Memory cleared for agent: {self.name}. Fresh and fierce!")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def get_info(self) -> Dict[str, str]:
        """Return this agent's press kit."""
        return {
            "name": self.name,
            "personality": self.personality,
            "capabilities": ", ".join(self.capabilities),
            "specialization": self.get_specialization(),
            "description": self.get_system_prompt().split('\n')[0],
            "tools": ", ".join(self.toolkit.list_tools())
        }

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
@app.route("/", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def index():
    response = ""
    if request.method == "POST":
        user_input = request.form.get("user_input", "")
        result = halo.process_input(user_input, source="gui")
        response = result.get("message", "")
    return render_template("index.html", response=response)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def run_cli():
    """Runs the Command-Line Interface for Halo."""
    print(f"[{halo.identity.name}] CLI is ready. Type 'exit' to quit.")
    while True:
        try:
            user_input = input(f"{halo.identity.name}> ")
            if user_input.lower() == "exit":
                print("Exiting Halo CLI.")
                break
            result = halo.process_input(user_input, source="cli")
            print(result["message"])
        except (KeyboardInterrupt, EOFError):
            print("\nExiting Halo CLI.")
            break

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class Halo:
    def __init__(self):
        self.identity = HaloIdentity()
        self.core = HaloCore(self)
        self.nexus = HaloNexus(self.core)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def process_input(self, user_input: str, source="cli") -> Dict[str, str]:
        self.nexus.route_input(user_input, source)
        response = self.nexus.last_response or self._handle_task(user_input)
        self.nexus.last_response = response
        self.nexus.update_context("last_task", user_input)
        return {"status": "success", "message": response}

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _handle_task(self, input_data: str) -> str:
        task_type, args = self._determine_task_type(input_data)
        handlers = {
            "math": self._handle_math,
            "trivia": self._handle_trivia,
            "store_fact": self._store_fact,
            "get_fact": self._get_fact,
            "status": self._handle_status,
            "learn": self._handle_learn,
            "apply": self._handle_apply,
            "default": self._handle_default
        }
        handler = handlers.get(task_type, self._handle_default)
        return handler(args)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _determine_task_type(self, user_input: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
        user_input_lower = user_input.lower().strip()
        if re.search(r'(\d+)\s*([\+\-\*/])\s*(\d+)', user_input_lower):
            return "math", user_input
        elif "who is" in user_input_lower or "what is" in user_input_lower:
            return "trivia", user_input
        elif user_input_lower.startswith("store fact"):
            return "store_fact", user_input.replace("store fact", "").strip()
        elif user_input_lower.startswith("get fact"):
            return "get_fact", user_input.replace("get fact", "").strip()
        elif user_input_lower.startswith("status"):
            return "status", user_input
        elif user_input_lower.startswith("learn"):
            return "learn", user_input.replace("learn", "", 1).strip()
        elif user_input_lower.startswith("apply"):
            return "apply", user_input.replace("apply", "", 1).strip()
        return "default", user_input

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _handle_math(self, input_data: str) -> str:
        try:
            match = re.search(r'(\d+)\s*([\+\-\*/])\s*(\d+)', input_data)
            if not match: return "Invalid math expression format."
            
            num1, op, num2 = int(match.group(1)), match.group(2), int(match.group(3))
            
            if op == '+': return f"Result: {num1 + num2}"
            if op == '-': return f"Result: {num1 - num2}"
            if op == '*': return f"Result: {num1 * num2}"
            if op == '/':
                return f"Result: {num1 / num2:.2f}" if num2 != 0 else "Error: Cannot divide by zero."
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Math error: {str(e)}"
        return "Unsupported math operation."

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _handle_trivia(self, input_data: str) -> str:
        return f"{self.identity.name} knows the cosmos! For example, a day on Venus is longer than its year."

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _store_fact(self, fact_data: str) -> str:
        try:
            key, value = fact_data.split("=", 1)
            key, value = key.strip(), value.strip()
            self.core.memory.store_memory(key, value)
            return f"Stored fact: '{key}'"
        except ValueError:
            return "Invalid format. Use: store fact key = value"

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _get_fact(self, key: str) -> str:
        memories = self.nexus.fetch_memory(key.strip(), num_results=1)
        return memories[0] if memories else f"Fact '{key}' not found."

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _handle_status(self, input_data: str) -> str:
        self.nexus.sync_modules()
        report = self.nexus.get_status_report()
        return f"Status Report: {report}"

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _handle_learn(self, task: str) -> str:
        return self.core.learning.meta_learn(task, task)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _handle_apply(self, task: str) -> str:
        return self.core.learning.apply_meta_knowledge(task)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def _handle_default(self, input_data: str) -> str:
        return f"I am {self.identity.name} ({self.identity.version}). Ready for your command. Try math ('5 * 3'), storing facts, or learning."

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class NeuralReasoner(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, input_size=384, hidden_size=20, output_size=1):
        super(NeuralReasoner, self).__init__()
        self.model = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(input_size, hidden_size),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(hidden_size, output_size)
        )
    def forward(self, x): return self.model(x)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class MemoryModule:
    def __init__(self): self.memory = {}
    def recall_memories(self, query, num_results=3): return [v for k, v in self.memory.items() if query.lower() in k.lower()][:num_results]
    def store_memory(self, key, value): self.memory[key] = value
    def is_ready(self): return True

    def is_active(self): return False # Placeholder

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class EthosModule:
    def validate_task(self, task):
        harmful_keywords = ["harm", "destroy", "kill"]
        return not any(keyword in task.lower() for keyword in harmful_keywords)
    def is_enforced(self): return True

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class OrchestratorModule:
    def __init__(self): self.task_queue = deque()
    def add_objective(self, task, source="gui"): self.task_queue.append({"task": task, "source": source})
    def is_operational(self): return True

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class LearningModule:
    def __init__(self, core):
        self.core = core
        self.model = NeuralReasoner(input_size=384)
        self.optimizer = torch.optim.Adam(self.model.parameters(), lr=0.01)
        self.loss_fn = nn.MSELoss()
        self.sentence_model = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')
        self.meta_knowledge = {}
    
    def meta_learn(self, task: str, data: str) -> str:
        task_key = f"meta_task_{task.lower()}"
        self.meta_knowledge[task_key] = data
        self.core.memory.store_memory(task_key, data)
        self.core.nexus.log_event(f"MAML-sim: Stored learning data for task '{task}'")
        return f"Halo has learned the procedure for task: {task}"

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def apply_meta_knowledge(self, task: str) -> str:
        task_key = f"meta_task_{task.lower()}"
        if task_key in self.meta_knowledge:
            return f"Applying learned procedure for '{task}': {self.meta_knowledge[task_key]}"
        return "No meta-knowledge for this task."
    
    def is_ready(self): return True

class HaloCore:

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class HaloNexus:
    def __init__(self, halo_core: 'HaloCore'):
        self.core = halo_core
        self.context = {}
        self.last_input = None
        self.last_response = None
        self.module_status = {}
        self.event_log = []

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def update_context(self, key, value):
        self.context[key] = value
        self.log_event(f"Context updated: {key} = {value}")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def route_input(self, input_text, source="gui"):
        self.last_input = input_text
        self.log_event(f"Input received from {source}: {input_text}")
        if self.core.ethos.validate_task(input_text):
            # The main halo._handle_task will now correctly dispatch learn/apply
            self.core.orchestrator.add_objective(input_text, source=source)
            # The response is generated by the main Halo class now
            self.last_response = None 
        else:
            self.last_response = "Directive vetoed. Ethical constraint triggered."
            self.core.voice.say(self.last_response, color="#FF0000")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def fetch_memory(self, query, num_results=3):
        memories = self.core.memory.recall_memories(query, num_results)
        self.log_event(f"Memory recall for '{query}': {len(memories)} results")
        return memories

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def get_status_report(self):
        self.sync_modules()
        return {
            "Awareness": self.core.awareness_level,
            "TasksInQueue": len(self.core.orchestrator.task_queue),
            "Modules": self.module_status,
            "Context": self.context,
        }

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def log_event(self, message):
        timestamp = time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        self.event_log.append(f"[{timestamp}] {message}")
        if len(self.event_log) > 500: # Keep log from growing infinitely
            self.event_log.pop(0)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
def sync_modules(self):
        self.module_status = {
            "Memory": self.core.memory.is_ready(),
            "Vision": self.core.vision.is_active(),
            "Voice": self.core.voice.is_ready(),
            "Ethos": self.core.ethos.is_enforced(),
            "Orchestrator": self.core.orchestrator.is_operational(),
            "Learning": self.core.learning.is_ready(),
        }
        self.log_event("Module status synced.")

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class Intent(enum.Enum):
    UNKNOWN, QUERY, COMMAND, AFFIRMATION, SALUTATION = range(5)

# --- Extracted from ARK-CONVO1.5.TXT ---
class IntentClassificationNexus:
    def classify(self, directive: str) -> Intent:
        lower_directive = directive.lower()
        if any(q in lower_directive for q in ['?', 'what', 'who', 'where', 'why', 'how', 'report', 'status']):
            return Intent.QUERY
        if any(c in lower_directive for c in ['clear', 'run', 'execute', 'create', 'do', 'make', 'diagnose']):
            return Intent.COMMAND
        if any(s in lower_directive for s in ['hello', 'greetings', 'goodbye', 'farewell']):
            return Intent.SALUTATION
        return Intent.AFFIRMATION

class SanctumCore(App):
    TITLE = "Nexus Halo"; SUB_TITLE = "The Resonant Voice v9.1"
    BINDINGS = [("q", "quit", "Quit")]
    def __init__(self, voice_q: asyncio.Queue, cog_q: asyncio.Queue, log_q: asyncio.Queue, locator: ResourceLocatorNexus, nexus: CognitiveNexus):
        super().__init__()
        self.voice_queue = voice_q; self.cognitive_queue = cog_q; self.log_queue = log_q
        self.locator = locator; self.nexus = nexus; self.log_widget: Log | None = None
    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
        yield Header(show_clock=True); yield Log(id="log"); yield Input(placeholder="Issue your directive, Architect...", id="input"); yield Footer()
    async def on_mount(self) -> None:
        self.log_widget = self.query_one(Log)
        css_path = self.locator.get_path("Shells/sanctum.css")
        if css_path.exists(): self.styles.read_and_watch(css_path)
        asyncio.create_task(audio_transmutation_worker(self.voice_queue, self.log_queue))
        asyncio.create_task(cognitive_worker(self.cognitive_queue, self.nexus))
        asyncio.create_task(self.log_worker())
        await self.voice_queue.put("Resonance achieved. Action protocols restored. The shell is complete.")
    async def on_input_submitted(self, message: Submitted):
        self.log_widget.write_line(f">> Architect: {message.value}"); self.query_one(Input).clear(); await self.cognitive_queue.put(message.value)
    async def log_worker(self):
        while True:
            message = await self.log_queue.get()
            if self.log_widget: self.log_widget.write_line(message)
            self.log_queue.task_done()

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class QuantumEntanglementTaskProtocol:
    """
    QETP-1.0: Manages high-value target (HVT) assignments via simulated
    quantum entanglement, allowing instantaneous consensus among a subset
    of nanites (the 'Entangled Cohort') regardless of distance or signal latency.
    This module overrides standard SEEK logic for HVTs.
    """
    
    HVT_THRESHOLD: float = 10.0 # A target mass or energy exceeding this value is HVT
    
    def __init__(self, hive_id: str):
        self.hive_id = hive_id
        # {HVT_id: Nanite_id} -> The nanite that currently holds the non-local 'key'
        self.hvt_assignment: Dict[int, int] = {}
        # List of nanite IDs registered to participate in QETP
        self.entangled_cohort: List[int] = []

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def register_nanite(self, nanite_id: int):
        """Adds a nanite to the cohort."""
        if nanite_id not in self.entangled_cohort:
            self.entangled_cohort.append(nanite_id)
            print(f"[QETP] Nanite N{nanite_id} entangled and ready for HVT assignment.")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def check_hvt_designation(self, target_atom_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """Determines if a target qualifies as a High-Value Target (HVT)."""
        return target_atom_data.get('mass', 0) >= self.HVT_THRESHOLD

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def instantaneous_assignment(self, nanite_id: int, hvt_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """
        Non-local assignment mechanism for an HVT. 
        Only nanites in the Entangled Cohort can attempt to 'claim' the key.
        This uses a deterministic priority based on ID (simulating a quantum key release).
        
        If the HVT is unassigned, the nanite with the lowest ID instantly receives the task.
        """
        hvt_id = hvt_data['id']
        
        if hvt_id not in self.hvt_assignment:
            # Check if this nanite is the lowest ID in the cohort
            eligible_cohort = [n_id for n_id in self.entangled_cohort if n_id > -1]
            
            if not eligible_cohort:
                return False # No nanites ready
                
            lowest_id = min(eligible_cohort)
            
            if nanite_id == lowest_id:
                # Instantaneous, non-contending claim
                self.hvt_assignment[hvt_id] = nanite_id
                print(f"[QETP ASSIGN] N{nanite_id} instantly claimed HVT A{hvt_id} via quantum priority key.")
                return True
            else:
                return False # Must yield to lower ID nanite
        
        # If already assigned, check if I am the assigned nanite
        return self.hvt_assignment.get(hvt_id) == nanite_id

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def release_assignment(self, hvt_id: int):
        """Releases the HVT assignment key, making it available again."""
        if hvt_id in self.hvt_assignment:
            del self.hvt_assignment[hvt_id]
            print(f"[QETP RELEASE] HVT A{hvt_id} key released for reassignment.")
