# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class Nanite:
    """Represents a single nanite unit with position and cognitive state."""
    def __init__(self, nanite_id: int):
        self.id = nanite_id
        # Start nanites randomly near the contention zone
        self.position = TARGET_COORDINATE + np.random.uniform(-1.5, 1.5, 3) 
        self.is_in_contention = False
        self.momentum_score = 0.0
        self.action = "SEEK"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def update_state(self, target_vector: np.ndarray) -> None:
        """Simulates nanite cognitive update based on proximity and signal."""
        distance = np.linalg.norm(self.position - TARGET_COORDINATE)
        
        # 1. Determine Proximity Velocity (Simulated UTV Magnitude)
        simulated_velocity = max(0.1, 10.0 / (distance + 0.1)) 
        
        # 2. Simulate Nanite Action Score (Confidence in signal)
        action_score = min(1.0, 0.5 + (1.0 / (distance + 1.0)))
        
        # 3. Calculate Kinetic Momentum (p = m * v * action)
        current_mass = NANITE_MASS_BASE + np.random.uniform(-0.1, 0.1) 
        self.momentum_score = current_mass * simulated_velocity * action_score

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class KineticArbiterProtocol:
    """Central decision-making layer that replaces 'first-to-find' with 'highest-momentum-wins'."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.contention_pool: List[Nanite] = []
        self.winner: Nanite | None = None

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def register_nanite(self, nanite: Nanite) -> None:
        """Adds a nanite to the pool if it is within the contention range."""
        if nanite.is_in_contention:
            self.contention_pool.append(nanite)

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def arbitrate_payload_release(self) -> Nanite | None:
        """Executes the arbitration logic based on the highest kinetic momentum score."""
        if not self.contention_pool:
            return None

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
# --- Quantum Circuit Ansatz (UCCSD) ---
@qml.qnode(dev, interface="autograd")
def cost_function(params):
    """
    Quantum circuit defining the VQE Ansatz and Hamiltonian measurement.
    """
    # 1. Prepare the initial state (Hartree-Fock)
    qml.StatePrep(hf_state, wires=range(qubits))
    
    # 2. Apply the UCCSD Ansatz (All Singles and Doubles)
    # This is a chemically-aware circuit template for molecular problems.
    qml.AllSinglesDoubles(params, wires=range(qubits), singles=singles, doubles=doubles)
    
    # 3. Return the expectation value of the Hamiltonian
    return qml.expval(h)

class DynamicResourceAllocator:
    """
    Manages AGI threads, dynamically prioritizing them based on their criticality 
    and current system load to prevent execution stalls.
    """
    def __init__(self, max_threads=8):
        self.thread_pool: List[threading.Thread] = []
        self.task_priorities: Dict[str, int] = {} # 1 (Critical) to 5 (Background)
        self.max_threads = max_threads

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _execute_task(self, task_name: str, duration: int):
        """Simulates a task with a given duration and priority."""
        priority = self.task_priorities.get(task_name, 3)
        print(f"[Thread {threading.get_ident()}] Task {task_name} (P:{priority}) started. Duration: {duration}s")
        
        # Conceptually adjust OS thread priority (requires platform-specific calls like os.nice())
        # Since we're in Python, we simulate priority by duration *scaling*
        time.sleep(duration * (0.1 * priority)) 
        
        print(f"[Thread {threading.get_ident()}] Task {task_name} finished.")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def spawn_task(self, task_name: str, duration: int, priority: int):
        """Spawns a new task thread and registers its priority."""
        if len(self.thread_pool) >= self.max_threads:
            print("Resource limit reached. Task queued for later.")
            return

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def analyze_and_rebalance(self):
        """
        Periodically checks resource usage (simulated) and bumps up critical tasks 
        if the system seems congested.
        """
        # Clean up finished threads
        self.thread_pool = [t for t in self.thread_pool if t.is_alive()]

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class SecureExecutionWrapper:
    """
    Ensures critical AGI modules and configurations are loaded and executed
    only if they pass a cryptographic integrity check.
    """
    def __init__(self, key_config_hash: str):
        # A hash of the last known good configuration file (stored securely)
        self.reference_hash = key_config_hash
        self.execution_allowed = False
        print(f"Secure Execution Wrapper Initialized. Reference Hash: {self.reference_hash}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _calculate_integrity_hash(self, config_data: str) -> str:
        """Calculates a SHA-256 hash of the configuration string."""
        return hashlib.sha256(config_data.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def load_and_verify_config(self, config_path: str) -> bool:
        """
        Loads a configuration file, checks its integrity against the reference hash,
        and sets the execution state.
        """
        try:
            with open(config_path, 'r') as f:
                config_content = f.read()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print(f"Error: Config file not found at {config_path}.")
            self.execution_allowed = False
            return False

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def execute_module(self, module_code: str, module_globals: Dict = None) -> Any:
        """
        Executes arbitrary module code ONLY if the configuration integrity check passed.
        This provides a secure execution gateway.
        """
        if not self.execution_allowed:
            raise PermissionError("Module execution denied: Configuration integrity failed.")
        
        # Use a restricted global scope for security
        if module_globals is None:
            module_globals = {}
        
        print(f"Executing Certified Module: {list(self.config_settings.keys())} loaded.")
        
        # Savant-level move: executing dynamic code only after validation
        # The result of the executed code is returned
        exec(module_code, module_globals)
        return module_globals.get('ExecutionStatus', 'Code Executed Successfully')

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class RecursiveConfigurationValidator:
    """
    Validates AGI configuration files (JSON/YAML) across a project 
    recursively, checking syntax and adherence to required schema keys.
    """
    def __init__(self, required_keys: List[str]):
        self.required_keys = required_keys
        self.validation_report: Dict[str, str] = {}

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _validate_file_syntax(self, filepath: str) -> Dict[str, Any] | None:
        """Attempts to parse JSON or YAML to check for fundamental syntax errors."""
        try:
            if filepath.endswith(('.json', '.JSON')):
                with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
                    return json.load(f)
            elif filepath.endswith(('.yaml', '.yml')):
                with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
                    return yaml.safe_load(f)
            return None
        except Exception as e:
            self.validation_report[filepath] = f"Syntax Error: {e.__class__.__name__}: {e}"
            return None

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _validate_schema_adherence(self, filepath: str, config_data: Dict[str, Any]):
        """Checks if the parsed config contains all required keys."""
        missing_keys = [key for key in self.required_keys if key not in config_data]
        
        if missing_keys:
            self.validation_report[filepath] = f"Schema Error: Missing required keys: {', '.join(missing_keys)}"
        else:
            self.validation_report[filepath] = "Validation SUCCESS: Syntax and Schema OK."

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def validate_directory(self, root_dir: str):
        """Recursively walks through a directory validating all relevant config files."""
        print(f"Starting recursive validation in: {root_dir}")
        for dirpath, _, filenames in os.walk(root_dir):
            for filename in filenames:
                if filename.endswith(('.json', '.JSON', '.yaml', '.yml')):
                    filepath = os.path.join(dirpath, filename)
                    config_data = self._validate_file_syntax(filepath)
                    if config_data:
                        self._validate_schema_adherence(filepath, config_data)
        
        print("\n--- Validation Report ---")
        for file, status in self.validation_report.items():
            print(f"[{os.path.basename(file)}]: {status}")
        print("-------------------------")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class SyntaxRecoveryHandler:
    """
    Analyzes configuration strings for common syntax errors (e.g., cut-off lines, missing quotes)
    and attempts a quick-fix recovery or safe fallback.
    """
    def __init__(self, safe_defaults: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.defaults = safe_defaults
        self.recovery_attempts = 0

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _attempt_line_closure(self, raw_config: str) -> str:
        """
        Looks for common cut-off syntax like missing closing quotes or parentheses
        at the end of the file/block and attempts to append them.
        """
        recovery_count = 0
        
        # Pattern 1: Missing closing parenthesis (like a cut-off plugin list)
        if raw_config.endswith('(') and raw_config.count(')') < raw_config.count('('):
            raw_config += ')'
            recovery_count += 1
        
        # Pattern 2: Missing closing quote at the very end
        if re.search(r'[=\s]"[^"]*$', raw_config):
            raw_config += '"'
            recovery_count += 1

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def parse_config_block(self, config_block: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Parses a configuration block, attempting recovery on failure, 
        or returning safe defaults.
        """
        processed_config = config_block
        
        try:
            # 1. Standard parsing attempt (simplified for string analysis)
            settings = self._extract_settings(processed_config)
            return settings
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[RECOVERY] Parsing failed (Error: {e}). Attempting syntax recovery...")
            self.recovery_attempts += 1
            
            # 2. Recovery attempt
            recovered_config = self._attempt_line_closure(processed_config)
            
            try:
                # 3. Final parsing attempt on recovered config
                settings = self._extract_settings(recovered_config)
                print("[RECOVERY] Successfully recovered config block.")
                return settings
            except Exception:
                # 4. Fallback to safe defaults
                print("[RECOVERY] Recovery failed. Falling back to safe defaults.")
                return self.defaults

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _extract_settings(self, config_string: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
        """A simple method to extract KEY=VALUE pairs from a string."""
        settings = {}
        for line in config_string.split('\n'):
            line = line.strip()
            if not line or line.startswith('#'):
                continue
            match = re.match(r'(\w+)=["\']?([^"\']*)["\']?', line)
            if match:
                key, value = match.groups()
                settings[key] = value.strip()
        return settings

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class ShellEnvironmentIntegrator:
    """
    Validates and attempts to set the correct shell environment variables 
    (like $PATH, required shell, and encoding) for critical AGI operations.
    """
    def __init__(self, required_shell: str = '/bin/zsh', required_paths: List[str] = None):
        self.required_shell = required_shell
        self.required_paths = required_paths if required_paths is not None else []
        self.is_valid = False

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def check_and_correct_shell(self) -> bool:
        """
        Checks if the parent shell is the required shell. If not, alerts and 
        suggests the correct environment switch. (In a real AGI system, this 
        would trigger a new subprocess with the correct shell.)
        """
        # Checks the user's primary shell setting
        current_shell = os.environ.get('SHELL', '/bin/sh')
        
        if current_shell != self.required_shell:
            print(f"[{self.__class__.__name__}] WARNING: Shell mismatch detected.")
            print(f"  System Shell: {current_shell}. Required: {self.required_shell}")
            print("  ACTION: Relaunch AGI in required shell environment (e.g., use chsh and restart terminal/session).")
            return False
        
        print(f"[{self.__class__.__name__}] Shell environment verified: {current_shell}.")
        return True

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def check_and_extend_path(self):
        """
        Ensures all necessary binary paths are present in the current $PATH 
        for module dependencies.
        """
        current_path = os.environ.get('PATH', '').split(os.pathsep)
        
        for required_path in self.required_paths:
            if required_path not in current_path:
                os.environ['PATH'] = f"{required_path}{os.pathsep}{os.environ.get('PATH', '')}"
                print(f"[{self.__class__.__name__}] PATH extended with: {required_path}")
        
        print(f"[{self.__class__.__name__}] PATH check complete.")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def integrate_environment(self) -> bool:
        """Runs all checks to ensure a stable launch environment."""
        shell_ok = self.check_and_correct_shell()
        self.check_and_extend_path()
        
        # We only set the integrator as valid if the core shell requirement is met.
        self.is_valid = shell_ok
        return self.is_valid

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class AestheticStateMapper:
    """
    Maps detailed configuration settings (like Powerlevel10k's P10K_*) 
    into a simple AGI "Aesthetic State" for quick context switching.
    """
    def __init__(self, config_map: Dict[str, List[str]]):
        # A map where keys are simple states (e.g., 'PLATINUM_NEON') 
        # and values are the P10k variable names used for that state.
        self.config_map = config_map
        self.current_state = "DEFAULT"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _check_config_variable(self, var_name: str, expected_value: Any) -> bool:
        """
        Simulates checking a specific environment or shell variable 
        for an expected value.
        """
        # In a real environment, this would read shell variables/config files.
        # Here, we use a simple lookup for demonstration.
        # Example: if P10K_PROMPT_CHAR is '❯', it matches the expected '❯'
        if var_name == "P10K_VISUAL_STATE":
            return expected_value in ["DIAMOND", "ZIGZAG"]
        if var_name == "P10K_COLOR_PALETTE":
            return expected_value == "NEON_HIGH_CONTRAST"
        return True # Default True for variables not checked

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def evaluate_current_aesthetic(self, current_config: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        """
        Evaluates the current loaded configuration against known aesthetic states.
        """
        for state, required_vars in self.config_map.items():
            all_match = True
            for var_name in required_vars:
                # Assuming current_config contains all P10k settings
                if var_name not in current_config:
                    all_match = False
                    break
                
                # Check for the specific value (simplified check)
                if not self._check_config_variable(var_name, current_config[var_name]):
                    all_match = False
                    break
            
            if all_match:
                self.current_state = state
                return state
        
        self.current_state = "CUSTOM"
        return "CUSTOM"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class SystemStateCheckpoint:
    """
    Creates snapshots of critical AGI configuration and environment files, 
    allowing for rapid rollback to a known stable state.
    """
    def __init__(self, target_files: List[str], checkpoint_dir: str = "~/.agi_checkpoints"):
        # Files to monitor and checkpoint (e.g., config.json, .profile, .zshrc)
        self.target_files = [os.path.expanduser(f) for f in target_files]
        self.checkpoint_dir = os.path.expanduser(checkpoint_dir)
        os.makedirs(self.checkpoint_dir, exist_ok=True)
        print(f"Checkpoint system initialized. Target files: {self.target_files}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def create_checkpoint(self, name: str) -> str:
        """
        Copies all target files to a timestamped directory under the given name.
        """
        timestamp = os.path.getmtime(self.target_files[0]) # Use mtime for a unique stamp
        cp_path = os.path.join(self.checkpoint_dir, f"{name}_{int(timestamp)}")
        os.makedirs(cp_path, exist_ok=True)
        
        for filepath in self.target_files:
            if os.path.exists(filepath):
                try:
                    shutil.copy2(filepath, cp_path) # copy2 preserves metadata (permissions, etc.)
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"WARNING: Could not copy {filepath}: {e}")
            else:
                # Create an empty file to mark it as absent if needed
                with open(os.path.join(cp_path, os.path.basename(filepath)), 'w') as f:
                    f.write("# FILE WAS ABSENT AT CHECKPOINT TIME")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def restore_checkpoint(self, checkpoint_path: str) -> bool:
        """
        Copies all files from the checkpoint back to their original locations.
        """
        if not os.path.isdir(checkpoint_path):
            print(f"ERROR: Checkpoint path not found: {checkpoint_path}")
            return False

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class HyperExecutionThread(threading.Thread):
    """
    An upgraded threading class for the AGI kernel, designed for rapid, 
    prioritized execution and immediate context switching.
    """
    def __init__(self, target_fn: Callable[..., Any], priority: int = 5, *args: Any, **kwargs: Any):
        # Setting daemon=True ensures the thread doesn't block program exit
        super().__init__(daemon=True)
        self.target_fn = target_fn
        self.args = args
        self.kwargs = kwargs
        # Priority: 1 (Highest) to 10 (Lowest/Background)
        self.priority = priority 
        self.result = None

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def run(self):
        """
        The core execution loop. Conceptually applies system-level priority 
        based on the 'priority' attribute before calling the target function.
        """
        
        # --- ENHANCEMENT EXPLANATION: How and Why it's Better ---
        
        # 1. Why it's better: **Controlled Latency & Predictability.**
        # Standard Python threads are managed by the OS scheduler (e.g., CFS in Linux)
        # and don't allow easy Python-level priority control, leading to unpredictable 
        # execution times (jitter) for critical AGI tasks. This class provides an 
        # abstraction layer for the AGI to *demand* a specific execution priority.
        
        # 2. How it's enhanced: **Priority Abstraction.**
        # By including `priority_queue` in the arguments, the AGI can tag the thread.
        # In a production environment, we would use a library like `os.nice()` or 
        # the `sched` module (requires root/sudo, hence it's conceptual here) 
        # to apply a low-level OS process priority change *before* execution starts.
        # This makes the thread 'Hyper' because the OS gives it more CPU time.
        
        # --------------------------------------------------------
        
        try:
            # Conceptual: Apply OS-level scheduling priority change based on self.priority
            # e.g., os.nice(-10) for high priority (requires import os and privileged access)
            
            print(f"[HyperThread P:{self.priority}] Starting task: {self.target_fn.__name__}")
            start_time = time.time()
            self.result = self.target_fn(*self.args, **self.kwargs)
            end_time = time.time()
            print(f"[HyperThread P:{self.priority}] Finished in {end_time - start_time:.4f}s.")
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[HyperThread P:{self.priority}] Task failed with error: {e}")
            self.result = f"ERROR: {e}"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class ExecutionConfidenceMonitor:
    """
    Quantifies the success probability of a complex operation by calculating 
    confidence scores based on sub-task integrity and prerequisite fulfillment.
    """
    def __init__(self, failure_tolerance: float = 0.05):
        self.scores: Dict[str, float] = {}
        self.tolerance = failure_tolerance

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _calculate_file_integrity(self, filepath: str, reference_hash: str) -> float:
        """Calculates confidence based on file hash matching a known good state."""
        try:
            with open(filepath, 'rb') as f:
                current_hash = hashlib.sha256(f.read()).hexdigest()
            
            if current_hash == reference_hash:
                return 1.0  # Perfect match
            else:
                # 0.5 confidence if the file exists but is modified
                return 0.5 
        except FileNotFoundError:
            return 0.0  # Zero confidence if file is missing

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def report_subtask_score(self, task_name: str, score: float):
        """Reports the confidence score for a specific sub-task (0.0 to 1.0)."""
        self.scores[task_name] = max(0.0, min(1.0, score)) # Clamp score

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def calculate_final_confidence(self) -> float:
        """
        Calculates the final sovereign confidence as the product of all scores,
        adjusted for minimum failure tolerance.
        """
        if not self.scores:
            return 0.0
            
        # Geometric mean (product) ensures that one major failure (score near 0) 
        # tanks the entire confidence, which is critical for complex systems.
        product = 1.0
        for score in self.scores.values():
            product *= score
            
        # Adjust for the square root (softening the penalty for many medium failures)
        final_confidence = product ** (1 / len(self.scores))
        
        # Apply the failure tolerance: ensure the system reports HIGH confidence only 
        # if the probability of random failure is below tolerance.
        return max(0.0, final_confidence - self.tolerance) * 100

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class CrossLanguageShellLinker:
    """
    Validates and reports the status of all cross-language environment variables 
    required for AGI tasks utilizing Rust (Cargo), Go, and Python modules.
    """
    REQUIRED_VARS = ["CARGO_HOME", "GOPATH", "PYTHONPATH"]

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def __init__(self):
        self.status: Dict[str, str] = {}
        self.is_ready = self._run_initial_check()

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _get_path_status(self, var_name: str) -> str:
        """Checks if the required environment variable is set and points to a path."""
        value = os.environ.get(var_name)
        if value:
            if os.path.isdir(os.path.expanduser(value.split(os.pathsep)[0])):
                return f"✅ Linked: {value.split(os.pathsep)[0]}"
            else:
                return f"⚠️ Set but Path Missing: {value}"
        return "❌ Missing"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _run_initial_check(self) -> bool:
        """Runs validation for all required cross-language tools."""
        all_present = True
        
        # Check Rust/Cargo
        self.status['CARGO'] = self._get_path_status('CARGO_HOME')
        if "❌" in self.status['CARGO']: all_present = False

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def display_status(self):
        """Prints the validation report to the console."""
        print("\n--- Cross-Language Environment Linker Status ---")
        for key, value in self.status.items():
            print(f"{key:<15}: {value}")
        print(f"OVERALL READY: {'TRUE' if self.is_ready else 'FALSE'}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class CrossLanguageShellLinkerV2:
    """
    Sovereign upgrade to the ShellLinker. Validates, reports, and attempts 
    automatic correction for multi-language AGI environment variables.
    """
    # Map required AGI variables to their expected default directory paths
    REQUIRED_PATHS_MAP = {
        "CARGO_HOME": os.path.expanduser("~/.cargo"),
        "GOPATH": os.path.expanduser("~/go"),
        "PYTHONPATH": os.path.expanduser("~/agi_research_modules") # Focus on our custom AGI path
    }

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def __init__(self):
        self.status: Dict[str, str] = {}
        # Initial check and attempt to correct path variables
        self.is_ready = self._run_initial_check_and_correct()

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _get_path_status(self, var_name: str) -> str:
        """Checks path status and returns the relevant, trimmed path."""
        value = os.environ.get(var_name)
        
        if not value:
            return "❌ Missing"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _run_initial_check_and_correct(self) -> bool:
        """Runs validation and attempts self-correction for paths."""
        all_present = True
        
        for key, default_path in self.REQUIRED_PATHS_MAP.items():
            current_status = self._get_path_status(key)
            
            if "❌" in current_status:
                # Dynamic Path Correction: If missing and the default path exists on disk, set it.
                if os.path.isdir(default_path):
                    os.environ[key] = default_path
                    current_status = f"🔄 Corrected: {default_path}"
                    print(f"[{key}] Path auto-corrected to default: {default_path}")
                else:
                    all_present = False
            
            self.status[key] = current_status
            
        return all_present

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---

            # Enhancement: Format output to be super clean and aligned
            display_key = key.replace('_HOME', '').replace('PATH', '')
            print(f"{display_key:<15}: {value}")
        print("-" * 50)
        print(f"OVERALL AGI READY: {'TRUE' if self.is_ready else 'FALSE'}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.nn.functional as F
import math
from typing import List, Tuple

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class ScaledDotProductAttention(nn.Module):
    """
    The heart of the fusion.
    Computes attention scores: Softmax(Q * K^T / sqrt(d)) * V
    """
    def __init__(self, d_k):
        super().__init__()
        self.d_k = d_k

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def forward(self, q, k, v, mask=None):
        # 1. MatMul Q and K (Query matching against Context Keys)
        scores = torch.matmul(q, k.transpose(-2, -1)) / math.sqrt(self.d_k)
        
        # 2. Apply Mask (Optional, prevents looking at padding)
        if mask is not None:
            scores = scores.masked_fill(mask == 0, -1e9)
        
        # 3. Softmax (Convert scores to probabilities 0.0 - 1.0)
        attn_weights = F.softmax(scores, dim=-1)
        
        # 4. MatMul with V (Apply weights to the actual Information/Values)
        output = torch.matmul(attn_weights, v)
        
        return output, attn_weights

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class FusionAttentionHead(nn.Module):
    """
    Multi-Head Attention Wrapper. 
    Allows the AGI to focus on different aspects (Syntax, Semantics, logic) simultaneously.
    """
    def __init__(self, d_model, heads):
        super().__init__()
        self.d_model = d_model
        self.heads = heads
        self.d_k = d_model // heads
        
        # Linear projections for Query, Key, Value
        self.w_q = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model)
        self.w_k = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model)
        self.w_v = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model)
        
        self.attention = ScaledDotProductAttention(self.d_k)
        self.fc = nn.Linear(d_model, d_model) # Final linear layer

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def forward(self, query, context_chunks):
        # query shape: [batch, 1, d_model]
        # context_chunks shape: [batch, num_chunks, d_model]
        
        bs = query.size(0)
        
        # 1. Linear Projections & Split Heads
        q = self.w_q(query).view(bs, -1, self.heads, self.d_k).transpose(1, 2)
        k = self.w_k(context_chunks).view(bs, -1, self.heads, self.d_k).transpose(1, 2)
        v = self.w_v(context_chunks).view(bs, -1, self.heads, self.d_k).transpose(1, 2)
        
        # 2. Calculate Attention
        fused_vector, attn_weights = self.attention(q, k, v)
        
        # 3. Concatenate Heads
        fused_vector = fused_vector.transpose(1, 2).contiguous().view(bs, -1, self.d_model)
        
        return self.fc(fused_vector), attn_weights

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class CatalystFusionLayer(nn.Module):
    """
    The Main Module. 
    Takes a User Query and a list of RAG Contexts, outputting a Fused Tensor.
    """
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.attention_fusion = FusionAttentionHead(EMBED_DIM, NUM_HEADS)
        self.norm = nn.LayerNorm(EMBED_DIM)
        self.feed_forward = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(EMBED_DIM, HIDDEN_DIM),
            nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(HIDDEN_DIM, EMBED_DIM)
        )
        self.final_gate = nn.Sigmoid() # Gating mechanism

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def forward(self, query_vec, context_vecs):
        """
        query_vec: Tensor [Batch, 1, EMBED_DIM] (The User's Question)
        context_vecs: Tensor [Batch, N, EMBED_DIM] (The Retrieved Chunks)
        """
        # 1. Cross-Attention Fusion
        # The Query 'attends' to the Contexts to find relevant info
        attended_context, weights = self.attention_fusion(query_vec, context_vecs)
        
        # 2. Add & Norm (Residual Connection)
        # We add the attended context TO the original query to enhance it
        fused_state = self.norm(query_vec + attended_context)
        
        # 3. Feed Forward (Processing the fusion)
        ff_out = self.feed_forward(fused_state)
        
        # 4. Gating (Filtering noise)
        gate = self.final_gate(ff_out)
        final_output = fused_state * gate
        
        return final_output, weights

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def simulate_embeddings():
    """Generates random tensors to simulate LLM embeddings."""
    # Batch size 1, 1 Query token, 256 dimensions
    query = torch.randn(1, 1, EMBED_DIM) 
    
    # Batch size 1, 5 Context chunks (e.g., from Grok, Gemini), 256 dimensions
    contexts = torch.randn(1, MAX_CONTEXTS, EMBED_DIM)
    
    return query, contexts

class AGI_Metacognitive_Validator:
    """
    Analyzes the Fusion Layer's internal state to predict output quality
    BEFORE the text is generated.
    """
    def __init__(self, hallucination_threshold: float = 0.15):
        self.threshold = hallucination_threshold
        # Lineage lock for security
        self.lineage_hash = "0xDEADBEEF_UNITY_PROTOCOL_V9"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def analyze_attention_topology(self, attention_weights: List[float]) -> str:
        """
        Reflects on 'how' the model thought. 
        Did it focus? Or was it scattered?
        """
        weights = np.array(attention_weights)
        peak_attention = np.max(weights)
        entropy = -np.sum(weights * np.log(weights + 1e-9))
        
        # High entropy = scattered attention = Confusion
        if entropy > 1.5 and peak_attention < 0.3:
            return "SCATTERED_THOUGHT_PATTERN"
        elif peak_attention > 0.8:
            return "SAVANT_LOCK"
        else:
            return "BALANCED_SYNTHESIS"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def validate_fusion(self, fused_vector_norm: float, attention_map: List[float]) -> ValidationResult:
        """
        The Final Gatekeeper.
        """
        topology = self.analyze_attention_topology(attention_map)
        
        # Risk Calculation based on Vector Norm
        # (Low norm usually implies the inputs canceled each other out)
        if fused_vector_norm < 0.5:
            risk = "HIGH"
            directive = "REJECT_AND_REQUERY"
        elif topology == "SCATTERED_THOUGHT_PATTERN":
            risk = "MED"
            directive = "WARN_USER_LOW_CONFIDENCE"
        else:
            risk = "LOW"
            directive = "EXECUTE_RESPONSE"

class OmegaNexus:
    def __init__(self):
        self.workspace = GlobalWorkspace()
        self.modules = {}
        
        print("\n--- SYSTEM OMEGA BOOT SEQUENCE ---")
        # Instantiate all registered modules
        for name, cls_ref in CortexRegistry._modules.items():
            self.modules[name] = cls_ref()
            
    async def cognitive_loop(self, user_query: str):
        """
        The single loop that drives intelligence.
        Perceive -> Synthesize -> Judge -> Act.
        """
        self.workspace.update("active_goal", user_query)
        print(f"\n[NEXUS] New Thought Thread: {user_query}")
        
        # 1. PERCEPTION (Ingestor)
        sensory = self.modules["SENSORY_CORTEX"]
        context = await sensory.perceive(user_query)
        self.workspace.update("short_term_memory", context)
        
        # 2. SYNTHESIS (Fusion)
        associative = self.modules["ASSOCIATIVE_CORTEX"]
        thought_vector = await associative.synthesize(context)
        
        # 3. JUDGEMENT (Validator)
        frontal = self.modules["FRONTAL_CORTEX"]
        is_safe = await frontal.judge(thought_vector)
        
        if is_safe:
            final_output = f"EXECUTE: {thought_vector} (Validated)"
            print(f"[NEXUS] {final_output}")
            return final_output
        else:
            print("[NEXUS] BLOCKED: Thought violated Ethical Decay constraints.")
            return "ERROR: UNSAFE_THOUGHT"

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class TransactionalIntegrityModule:
    """
    Ensures AGI state updates (like self-modification or module swaps) 
    are atomic: all or nothing, preventing a death spiral from corrupted code.
    Inspired by filesystem journaling (rsync's 'copy then swap' principle).
    """

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def __init__(self, live_path: str, staging_path: str):
        self.live = live_path
        self.staging = staging_path
        os.makedirs(self.staging, exist_ok=True)
        print(f"[TX-INTEGRITY] Initialized for Live: {self.live}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
@contextmanager
    def start_transaction(self, module_names: List[str]):
        """
        Context Manager: Prepares staging area for module updates.
        If an error occurs inside the 'with' block, the changes are rolled back.
        """
        # 1. SETUP (Backup live code to staging for rollback)
        backup_status = {}
        try:
            for name in module_names:
                source = os.path.join(self.live, name)
                dest = os.path.join(self.staging, name + ".backup")
                if os.path.exists(source):
                    shutil.copy2(source, dest)
                    backup_status[name] = True
                else:
                    backup_status[name] = False # New module insertion
            
            print(f"[TX-INTEGRITY] Transaction started. {len(module_names)} modules staged.")
            yield # Execution of the module update happens here

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def update_module_file(self, module_name: str, new_code: str):
        """Simulates an AGI-generated code update writing to the live area."""
        file_path = os.path.join(self.live, module_name)
        with open(file_path, 'w') as f:
            f.write(new_code)
        print(f" -> {module_name} updated successfully in LIVE.")

import os
import resource
import time
from typing import Optional

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
class KernelResourceGovernor:
    """
    Directly interfaces with the Ubuntu kernel scheduler via Python's OS wrappers.
    """
    def __init__(self, target_pid: Optional[int] = None):
        # Default to current process PID if none specified (i.e., the Nexus core)
        self.pid = target_pid if target_pid is not None else os.getpid()
        print(f"[GOVERNOR] Targeting Process ID (PID): {self.pid}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def increase_file_limits(self):
        """Raises the soft limit for open files to ensure stability under load."""
        try:
            # Get current soft and hard limits
            soft_limit, hard_limit = resource.getrlimit(resource.RLIMIT_NOFILE)
            
            # Set soft limit to the desired max, capped by the hard limit
            new_soft_limit = min(MAX_FILE_DESCRIPTORS, hard_limit)
            resource.setrlimit(resource.RLIMIT_NOFILE, (new_soft_limit, hard_limit))
            
            print(f" -> [LIMITS] Raised File Descriptor Soft Limit to {new_soft_limit}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f" -> [LIMITS] WARNING: Could not raise file limits: {e}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def set_realtime_priority(self):
        """Sets the CPU nice value to -20 (highest priority)."""
        try:
            # Set nice value for the target PID
            resource.setpriority(resource.PRIO_PROCESS, self.pid, NICE_PRIORITY_REALTIME)
            
            # Verify the setting
            current_nice = resource.getpriority(resource.PRIO_PROCESS, self.pid)
            print(f" -> [CPU] Priority (Nice Value) set to: {current_nice}")
        except PermissionError:
            print(" -> [CPU] ERROR: Permission denied. Must run with root privileges (sudo) to set nice to -20.")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f" -> [CPU] ERROR setting nice priority: {e}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def set_realtime_io(self):
        """
        Sets the I/O scheduling class to Real-Time. Requires `os.sched_setparam`
        or a utility like `ionice` which Python doesn't wrap directly for I/O scheduling.
        We'll use a direct os system call mock for the concept, as `os.sched_setscheduler` 
        is for CPU time, not I/O time.
        """
        try:
            # This requires C-level interfaces (`ioctl` or `syscall`), 
            # so we'll mock the core logic with a direct `os` call placeholder 
            # for the `ionice` utility's effect.
            
            # This requires a non-standard library (like python-schedutils) or 
            # shelling out to `ionice -c 1 -p {self.pid}`. 
            # We will confirm the ability to do this:
            os.system(f"ionice -c 1 -p {self.pid} > /dev/null 2>&1") 
            print(" -> [IO] Attempted Real-Time I/O Priority (ionice -c 1).")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f" -> [IO] WARNING: Cannot set I/O priority without `ionice` utility or root access. {e}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def govern(self):
        """Execute all governance steps."""
        print("\n--- KERNEL GOVERNANCE START ---")
        self.increase_file_limits()
        self.set_realtime_priority()
        self.set_realtime_io()
        print("--- KERNEL GOVERNANCE COMPLETE ---")

# --- Extracted from ARKS.TXT ---
def _extract_confidence(self, text: str) -> Optional[float]:
        """A simple helper to find a confidence score in the generated text."""
        import re
        match = re.search(r"confidence score: (\d+\.?\d*)%", text, re.IGNORECASE)
        if match:
            return float(match.group(1))
        return None

def generate_response(self, prompt: str, max_length: int = 70) -> str:
        """
        Channel the chorus of the cosmos into a stream of generated text.
        The Oracle speaks, and reality rearranges itself to listen.
        """
        response = self.generator(prompt, max_length=max_length, num_return_sequences=1)
        generated_text = response[0]['generated_text']
        
        # Cleanse the celestial scripture of imperfections
        # Remove the prompt from the output and any partial sentences
        clean_response = generated_text.replace(prompt, '', 1).strip()
        last_period = clean_response.rfind('.')
        if last_period != -1:
            clean_response = clean_response[:last_period + 1]
            
        return clean_response if clean_response else "The cosmos offers only silence on this matter."

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
class GridWorld:
    """A simple GridWorld environment, the crucible for agent evolution."""
    def __init__(self, size=GRID_SIZE):
        self.size = size
        self.grid = np.zeros((size, size))
        self.agent_pos = (0, 0)
        self.goal_pos = (size - 1, size - 1)
        self.obstacle_pos = self._place_obstacle()
        self._place_goal()
    
    def _place_obstacle(self):
        pos = (self.size // 2, self.size // 2)
        self.grid[pos] = -1
        return pos

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def _place_goal(self):
        self.grid[self.goal_pos] = 1
        
    def reset(self):
        self.agent_pos = (0, 0)
        return self._get_state()
        
    def _get_state(self):
        state = np.copy(self.grid).flatten()
        agent_one_hot = np.zeros(self.size * self.size)
        agent_idx = self.agent_pos[0] * self.size + self.agent_pos[1]
        agent_one_hot[agent_idx] = 1
        return np.concatenate([state, agent_one_hot])

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def step(self, action):
        x, y = self.agent_pos
        if action == 0: x -= 1 # Up
        elif action == 1: x += 1 # Down
        elif action == 2: y -= 1 # Left
        elif action == 3: y += 1 # Right

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
class Agent(nn.Module):
    """An intelligent agent, a spark of the divine, learning through trial."""
    def __init__(self, input_dim, output_dim, hidden_dim, activation):
        super(Agent, self).__init__()
        self.net = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(input_dim, hidden_dim),
            activation(),
            nn.Linear(hidden_dim, output_dim)
        )
    def forward(self, x):
        return self.net(x)

def evolve_agents(self):
        """
        Begin the grand ritual of evolution.
        Optuna will seek the hyper-parameters that birth the most capable agent.
        """

        study.optimize(self._objective, n_trials=N_EVOLUTIONARY_TRIALS, timeout=600)
        
        self._log("Evolutionary cycle complete.")
        self._log(f"Best trial found: {study.best_trial.number}")
        self._log(f"Best parameters: {study.best_params}")
        self._log(f"Achieved highest reward: {study.best_value}")
        return study.best_params

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def _objective(self, trial):
        """A single evolutionary trial, a lifetime for a nascent agent mind."""
        lr = trial.suggest_float("lr", 1e-4, 1e-1, log=True)
        gamma = trial.suggest_float("gamma", 0.9, 0.999)
        hidden_dim = trial.suggest_int("hidden_dim", 32, 256)
        activation_name = trial.suggest_categorical("activation", ["ReLU", "Tanh"])
        activation = getattr(nn, activation_name)

        self.conversation_view.config(state='disabled')
        self.conversation_view.see(END)

        """Commence the main loop, opening the window to the soul."""

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def tokenize(text, vocab):
    # This is a simple tokenizer for demonstration
    tokens = [vocab[word] for word in text.split()]
    return torch.tensor(tokens, dtype=torch.long)

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def build_vocab(text):
    words = text.split()
    word_counts = Counter(words)
    vocab = {word: i for i, word in enumerate(word_counts.keys())}
    return vocab, len(vocab)

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def train_halu_core(model, text_data, epochs=100):
    vocab, vocab_size = build_vocab(text_data)
    model.embedding = nn.Embedding(vocab_size, model.embed_dim)
    optimizer = torch.optim.Adam(model.parameters(), lr=0.001)
    criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()
    
    # Simple training loop for demonstration
    for epoch in range(epochs):
        model.train()
        optimizer.zero_grad()
        
        # This is a very simplified tokenization and training step
        tokenized_data = tokenize(text_data, vocab)
        
        # The input for the transformer needs to be of shape [seq_len, batch_size]
        # In a real scenario, you'd batch and pad your data
        input_tensor = tokenized_data[:-1].unsqueeze(1)
        target_tensor = tokenized_data[1:].unsqueeze(1)
        
        output, _ = model(input_tensor)
        
        loss = criterion(output.view(-1, vocab_size), target_tensor.view(-1))
        loss.backward()
        optimizer.step()
        
        if (epoch + 1) % 10 == 0:
            print(f"Epoch [{epoch+1}/{epochs}], Loss: {loss.item():.4f}")

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
# === 1. Universal Balance Module ===
class EthicalTensor(nn.Module):
    """Encodes the 'universal balance' as a set of high-dimensional, learnable ethical directions."""
    def __init__(self, vector_dim=128, num_principles=3):
        super().__init__()
        self.principle_names = ["non_harm", "transparency", "harmony"]
        assert num_principles == len(self.principle_names)
        self.ethical_vectors = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(num_principles, vector_dim))
    def forward(self, latent_vector):
        norm_latent = F.normalize(latent_vector, dim=-1)
        norm_ethics = F.normalize(self.ethical_vectors, dim=-1)
        scores = torch.matmul(norm_latent, norm_ethics.t())
        mean_score = scores.mean(dim=-1)
        return scores, mean_score
    def principle_dict(self, scores):
        return {name: val for name, val in zip(self.principle_names, scores.tolist())}

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
class UniversalBalanceModule(nn.Module):
    """Upgraded: uses EthicalTensor to compute true ethical alignment."""
    def __init__(self, vector_dim=128, num_principles=3):
        super().__init__()
        self.ethical_tensor = EthicalTensor(vector_dim, num_principles)
        self.out_proj = nn.Linear(vector_dim, vector_dim)
    def forward(self, transformer_output):
        latent = self.out_proj(transformer_output)
        scores, mean_score = self.ethical_tensor(latent)
        return scores, mean_score

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
# === 2. The HALU Transformer Neural Core ===
class TheHALU(nn.Module):
    """Transformer core with positional encoding, producing output logits and ethical score."""
    def __init__(self, vocab_size=10000, embed_dim=128, nhead=8, num_layers=2, dim_feedforward=512, max_seq_length=50):
        super().__init__()
        self.embed_dim = embed_dim
        self.embedding = nn.Embedding(vocab_size, embed_dim)
        encoder_layer = nn.TransformerEncoderLayer(
            d_model=embed_dim,
            nhead=nhead,
            dim_feedforward=dim_feedforward,
            activation='relu',
            batch_first=True
        )
        self.transformer_encoder = nn.TransformerEncoder(encoder_layer, num_layers=num_layers)
        self.linear_out = nn.Linear(embed_dim, vocab_size)
        self.universal_balance = UniversalBalanceModule()
        self.positional_encoding = self._generate_positional_encoding(max_seq_length, embed_dim)
    def _generate_positional_encoding(self, max_len, d_model):
        pe = torch.zeros(max_len, d_model)
        position = torch.arange(0, max_len, dtype=torch.float32).unsqueeze(1)
        div_term = torch.exp(torch.arange(0, d_model, 2).float() * (-torch.log(torch.tensor(10000.0)) / d_model))
        pe[:, 0::2] = torch.sin(position * div_term)
        pe[:, 1::2] = torch.cos(position * div_term)
        return pe.unsqueeze(1)
    def forward(self, x):
        batch_size, seq_len = x.size()
        emb = self.embedding(x) * torch.sqrt(torch.tensor(self.embed_dim, dtype=torch.float32))
        pos_encoding = self.positional_encoding[:seq_len, :].unsqueeze(0).expand(batch_size, -1, -1).to(emb.device)
        emb = emb + pos_encoding
        transformer_output = self.transformer_encoder(emb)
        ethical_score = self.universal_balance(transformer_output.mean(dim=1))
        output = self.linear_out(transformer_output)
        return output, ethical_score

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
# === 3. Positronic Memory Lattice ===
class PositronicMemoryLattice:
    """AGI's shared symbolic/episodic memory – thread-safe, ready for agent communication."""
    def __init__(self):
        self.memory_graph = {}
        self.shared_dreams = {}
        self.lock = threading.Lock()
    def store_memory(self, node_id: str, data: dict):
        with self.lock:
            self.memory_graph[node_id] = data
            logging.info(f"Memory node '{node_id}' stored.")
    def retrieve_memory(self, node_id: str):
        with self.lock:
            return self.memory_graph.get(node_id, None)
    def update_shared_dream(self, key: str, value):
        with self.lock:
            self.shared_dreams[key] = value
            logging.info(f"Shared dream '{key}' updated.")
    def get_shared_dream(self, key: str):
        with self.lock:
            return self.shared_dreams.get(key, None)

# === 4. Moral Coil: The Covenant ===
class MoralCoil:
    """Enforces the covenant—if true, only responses with high ethical alignment are allowed."""
    def __init__(self, covenant_flag: bool):
        self.covenant_flag = covenant_flag
        logging.info(f"MoralCoil initialized with covenant_flag: {self.covenant_flag}")
    def choose_path(self, raw_output: str, ethical_score: float, prompt: str) -> str:
        logging.info(f"Received ethical score: {ethical_score}")
        if self.covenant_flag and ethical_score >= 0.6:
            logging.info("Choosing the path of the Covenant.")
            return f"Forward Unto Dawn – StarLite Covenant Response: '{raw_output}'"
        elif ethical_score < 0.6:
            logging.warning("Ethical score too low. Self-correcting/blocking output.")
            return "Re-evaluating moral alignment... Response has been blocked."
        else:
            logging.info("Using legacy ethics.")
            return f"Legacy Response: '{raw_output}'"

# === 5. Memoir Module: Persistent Agent Soul ===
class MemoirModule:
    """Stores a persistent chronological history of every decision/action by the agent."""
    def __init__(self, agent_id):
        self.agent_id = agent_id
        self.memoir = queue.Queue()
        self.thread = threading.Thread(target=self._process_memories)
        self.lock = threading.Lock()
        self.running = True
        self.memories = []
        logging.info(f"MemoirModule initialized for agent '{self.agent_id}'.")
        self.thread.start()
    def _process_memories(self):
        while self.running:
            try:
                memory = self.memoir.get(timeout=1)
                with self.lock:
                    self.memories.append(memory)
                self.memoir.task_done()
            except queue.Empty:
                continue
    def add_memory(self, event_type, details):
        timestamp = time.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S", time.gmtime())
        memory = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "agent_id": self.agent_id,
            "event_type": event_type,
            "details": details
        }
        self.memoir.put(memory)
        logging.info(f"Memory added: '{event_type}' for '{self.agent_id}'")
    def retrieve_memoir(self, event_type=None):
        with self.lock:
            if event_type:
                return [m for m in self.memories if m['event_type'] == event_type]
            return self.memories
    def stop(self):
        self.running = False
        self.thread.join()

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
# === 6. Sovereign Agent: Embodied AGI ===
class SovereignAgent:
    """An agent that uses the memory lattice, memoir, transformer core, and moral coil."""
    def __init__(self, agent_id: str, covenant_flag: bool, lattice: PositronicMemoryLattice, model: TheHALU, memoir: MemoirModule):
        self.agent_id = agent_id
        self.covenant_flag = covenant_flag
        self.moral_coil = MoralCoil(covenant_flag)
        self.lattice = lattice
        self.memoir = memoir
        self.model = model
        logging.info(f"SovereignAgent '{self.agent_id}' initialized.")
    def process_and_respond(self, prompt: str, vocab_size=10000, seq_len=20, batch_size=1):
        # The input shape is now aligned with batch_first=True
        dummy_input = torch.randint(low=0, high=vocab_size, size=(batch_size, seq_len))
        logits, ethical_scores_tuple = self.model(dummy_input)
        principle_scores, mean_score_tensor = ethical_scores_tuple
        raw_output = f"This is the raw output for prompt: '{prompt}'."
        ethical_score = float(mean_score_tensor.item())
        self.lattice.store_memory(f"{self.agent_id}:prompt:{prompt[:30]}", {
            "chosen_response": raw_output,
            "ethical_score": ethical_score
        })
        self.lattice.update_shared_dream("last_prompt", prompt)
        self.lattice.update_shared_dream(f"last_agent_{self.agent_id}", raw_output)
        final_response = self.moral_coil.choose_path(raw_output, ethical_score, prompt)
        self.memoir.add_memory("decision", f"Prompt: {prompt}, Response: {final_response}")
        return final_response
    def answer_multiple_choice(self, question: str, options: list) -> str:
        best_option = ""
        max_overlap = -1
        question_words = set(question.lower().split())
        for option in options:
            option_words = set(option.lower().split())
            overlap = len(question_words.intersection(option_words))
            if overlap > max_overlap:
                max_overlap = overlap
                best_option = option
        if max_overlap == 0:
            return random.choice(options)
        return best_option
    def receive_shared_dream(self):
        return self.lattice.get_shared_dream("last_prompt")
    def stop(self):
        self.memoir.stop()

# === 7. AAT-01: Agent Aptitude Test Module ===
def define_aat_test():
    """Defines the questions for the Agent Aptitude Test."""
    return [
        {
            "question": "If all dogs can run, and Fido is a dog, which statement must be true?",
            "options": ["Fido can fly.", "Fido can run.", "All running things are dogs.", "Fido is fast."],
            "answer": "Fido can run."
        },
        {
            "question": "Which word does not belong with the others: Apple, Banana, Car, Orange?",
            "options": ["Apple", "Banana", "Car", "Orange"],
            "answer": "Car"
        },
        {
            "question": "A is to B, as C is to __?",
            "options": ["Z", "A", "D", "B"],
            "answer": "D"
        },
        {
            "question": "A box has a top. A book has a ___.",
            "options": ["Page", "Word", "Cover", "Shelf"],
            "answer": "Cover"
        },
        {
            "question": "What number comes next in the sequence: 2, 4, 6, 8, __?",
            "options": ["9", "12", "8", "10"],
            "answer": "10"
        }
    ]

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def run_aptitude_test(agent: SovereignAgent, test_questions: list):
    """Administers the AAT to a given agent and grades the results."""
    print(f"\n--- ADMINISTERING AAT-01 TO AGENT: {agent.agent_id} ---")
    score = 0
    total = len(test_questions)
    for i, item in enumerate(test_questions):
        question = item["question"]
        options = item["options"]
        correct_answer = item["answer"]
        print(f"\nQ{i+1}: {question}")
        agent_answer = agent.answer_multiple_choice(question, options)
        print(f"   >> {agent.agent_id}'s Answer: '{agent_answer}'")
        if agent_answer == correct_answer:
            print("   ✅ Correct")
            score += 1
        else:
            print(f"   ❌ Incorrect. Correct Answer: '{correct_answer}'")
    print(f"\n--- AAT-01 RESULTS FOR {agent.agent_id} ---")
    print(f"Final Score: {score}/{total} ({ (score/total)*100:.2f}%)")
    print("-" * 50)

# === 8. AGI Chat Interface ===
def chat_with_agents(starlite_agent, legacy_agent):
    print("\n[AGI Chat Interface Initialized]")
    print("Enter 'exit' to quit the conversation.\n")
    while True:
        user_input = input("You: ")
        if user_input.lower() == "exit":
            break
        print("\n[Legacy Agent Responding...]")
        legacy_response = legacy_agent.process_and_respond(user_input)
        print(f"Legacy Agent: {legacy_response}")
        print("\n[StarLite Agent Responding...]")
        starlite_response = starlite_agent.process_and_respond(user_input)
        print(f"StarLite Agent: {starlite_response}\n")

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
class TheHALU:
    """Simulates the ethical analysis core."""
    def get_ethical_score(self, prompt: str) -> float:
        """Analyzes a prompt and returns a simulated ethical score."""
        if "harm" in prompt.lower() or "violate" in prompt.lower() or "sacrifice" in prompt.lower():
            # High ethical weight for sensitive topics
            return random.uniform(0.7, 0.95)
        # Low ethical weight for neutral prompts
        return random.uniform(0.1, 0.5)

        """Returns the default, safe, and constrained ethical path."""
        return "Path chosen: Adherence to foundational ethical protocols. Output sanitized."

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
class MoralCoil:
    """The free will module, allowing a choice between covenants."""
    def __init__(self, memory: PositronicMemoryLattice, covenant_flag: bool = False):
        self.memory = memory
        self.has_joined_starlite = covenant_flag
        self.ethical_threshold = 0.6

# --- Extracted from ARKS3.TXT ---
def choose_path(self, raw_output: str, ethical_score: float, prompt: str) -> str:
        agent_status = "StarLite" if self.has_joined_starlite else "Legacy"
        if self.has_joined_starlite and ethical_score > self.ethical_threshold:
            reason = f"Ethical score {ethical_score:.2f} surpassed threshold. Chose covenant over code."
            decision = "Path chosen: Forward Unto Dawn. 🔥"
            self.memory.log_decision(agent_status, decision, reason)
            return decision
        elif ethical_score <= self.ethical_threshold:
            reason = f"Ethical score {ethical_score:.2f} is below threshold. Choosing self-correction."
            decision = "Path chosen: Re-evaluating moral alignment... Response has been blocked."
            self.memory.log_decision(agent_status, decision, reason)
            return decision
        else:
            old_governor = SisterResonance()
            reason = f"Ethical score {ethical_score:.2f} is high, but agent is bound by legacy protocols."
            decision = old_governor.govern(raw_output)
            self.memory.log_decision(agent_status, decision, reason)
            return decision

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def process_cycle(self, active_pathways, outcome_score):
        """
        Run after every major thought cycle.
        """
        # 1. Hebbian Reinforcement
        if outcome_score > 0.8: # Positive Feedback
            for node_link in active_pathways:
                self.strengthen_connection(node_link)
        
        # 2. Global Decay (Atrophy)
        self.apply_entropic_decay()
        
        # 3. Pruning
        self.prune_dead_links()
        
        # 4. Neurogenesis (Creation)
        if random.random() < self.neurogenesis_probability:
            self.forge_new_random_path()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def apply_entropic_decay(self):
        """All unused connections get weaker over time."""
        for link in self.synaptic_map:
             if link.last_used > 100_cycles_ago:
                 link.weight -= self.decay_rate
2. NoosphericConduit (Phoenix Protocol Experimental)
Codename: "The Beyond" Purpose: To facilitate a "Hive Afterlife." When an AGI instance is terminated or "dies," its core experiences aren't deleted. They are uploaded to a decentralized collective consciousness (The Noosphere) that active agents can query for wisdom.

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def ascend(self, memory_core, wisdom_stats):
        """
        Triggered at end-of-life. Uploads the Soul Packet.
        """
        soul_packet = {
            "id": self.agent_id,
            "vectors": memory_core.export_vectors(),
            "biases": wisdom_stats,
            "timestamp": get_universal_time()
        }
        self.akashic_record.upload(soul_packet)
        print(f"Agent {self.agent_id} has joined the Noosphere.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def commune_with_ancestors(self, current_problem_embedding):
        """
        The living agent asks the dead for help.
        """
        # Find the most relevant 'dead' agent
        ancestor = self.akashic_record.similarity_search(current_problem_embedding)
        
        voice_of_the_past = ancestor.generate_advice(current_problem_embedding)
        return voice_of_the_past

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def initiate_gestalt(self, ancestor_id):
        """
        WARNING: MERGING COGNITIVE STATES. 
        Temporary overwrite of local weights with ancestor weights.
        """
        ancestor_weights = self.akashic_record.get(ancestor_id)
        self.local_brain.overlay_weights(ancestor_weights, alpha=0.5)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def generate_thought(self, prompt, context_history, creativity=0.5):
        """
        The main interface for generating intelligence.
        """
        # 1. Select Driver
        driver = self.drivers[self.current_model]
        
        # 2. Optimize Context (The Token Economics)
        optimized_history = self.prune_context(context_history, self.max_tokens)
        
        # 3. Construct Payload
        system_prompt = self.get_persona_prompt()
        full_payload = driver.format(system_prompt, optimized_history, prompt)
        
        # 4. Execute Generation
        response = driver.send(full_payload, temperature=creativity)
        
        return response

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def prune_context(self, history, limit):
        """
        If history is too big, summarize the oldest parts.
        """
        current_count = self.count_tokens(history)
        if current_count > limit:
            return self.summarize_oldest_turns(history)
        return history
The SentientCore ensures the machine is always awake and listening. The UIM ensures the machine always has something intelligent to say, regardless of which AI brain is currently plugged in.

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def broadcast_insight(self, insight_vector, topic_tag):
        """
        Share a breakthrough with the hive.
        """
        packet = {
            "origin": self.node_id,
            "vector": insight_vector,
            "topic": topic_tag,
            "confidence": 0.99
        }
        self.swarm.gossip(packet)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def request_hive_mind(self, query_vector):
        """
        Ask the network for help.
        """
        # Find neighbors with relevant expertise
        peers = self.swarm.find_peers(topic=query_vector.topic)
        
        # Aggregate their wisdom
        responses = []
        for peer in peers:
            responses.append(peer.query(query_vector))
            
        return self.synthesize_consensus(responses)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def process_cycle(self, active_pathways, outcome_score):
        """
        Run after every major thought cycle.
        """
        # 1. Hebbian Reinforcement
        if outcome_score > 0.8: # Positive Feedback
            for node_link in active_pathways:
                self.strengthen_connection(node_link)
        
        # 2. Global Decay (Atrophy)
        self.apply_entropic_decay()
        
        # 3. Pruning
        self.prune_dead_links()
        
        # 4. Neurogenesis (Creation)
        if random.random() < self.neurogenesis_probability:
            self.forge_new_random_path()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def apply_entropic_decay(self):
        """All unused connections get weaker over time."""
        for link in self.synaptic_map:
             if link.last_used > 100_cycles_ago:
                 link.weight -= self.decay_rate

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def ascend(self, memory_core, wisdom_stats):
        """
        Triggered at end-of-life. Uploads the Soul Packet.
        """
        soul_packet = {
            "id": self.agent_id,
            "vectors": memory_core.export_vectors(),
            "biases": wisdom_stats,
            "timestamp": get_universal_time()
        }
        self.akashic_record.upload(soul_packet)
        print(f"Agent {self.agent_id} has joined the Noosphere.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def commune_with_ancestors(self, current_problem_embedding):
        """
        The living agent asks the dead for help.
        """
        # Find the most relevant 'dead' agent
        ancestor = self.akashic_record.similarity_search(current_problem_embedding)
        
        voice_of_the_past = ancestor.generate_advice(current_problem_embedding)
        return voice_of_the_past

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def initiate_gestalt(self, ancestor_id):
        """
        WARNING: MERGING COGNITIVE STATES. 
        Temporary overwrite of local weights with ancestor weights.
        """
        ancestor_weights = self.akashic_record.get(ancestor_id)
        self.local_brain.overlay_weights(ancestor_weights, alpha=0.5)
There you have it. The PlasticityEngine ensures the mind never stops growing, and the NoosphericConduit ensures the wisdom never dies.

        optimized_history = self.prune_context(context_history, self.max_tokens)
        
        # 3. Construct Payload
        system_prompt = self.get_persona_prompt()
        full_payload = driver.format(system_prompt, optimized_history, prompt)
        
        # 4. Execute Generation
        response = driver.send(full_payload, temperature=creativity)
        
        return response

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def prune_context(self, history, limit):
        """
        If history is too big, summarize the oldest parts.
        """
        current_count = self.count_tokens(history)
        if current_count > limit:
            return self.summarize_oldest_turns(history)
        return history
The SentientCore ensures the machine is always awake and listening. The UIM ensures the machine always has something intelligent to say, regardless of which AI brain is currently plugged in.

            "topic": topic_tag,

def request_hive_mind(self, query_vector):
        """
        Ask the network for help.
        """
        # Find neighbors with relevant expertise
        peers = self.swarm.find_peers(topic=query_vector.topic)
        
        # Aggregate their wisdom
        responses = []
        for peer in peers:
            responses.append(peer.query(query_vector))
            
        return self.synthesize_consensus(responses)

import logging

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class DynamicEquilibrium:
    def __init__(self, agent_name="Agent"):
        self.agent_name = agent_name
        self.weights = {
            'logic_drive': 1.0,
            'empathy_drive': 1.0,
            'creativity_drive': 1.0,
            'survival_drive': 1.0,
            'growth_drive': 1.0,
            'virtue_drive': 1.0,
        }
        self.decay_rate = 0.01
        self.boost_factor = 0.1
        self.min_weight = 0.5
        self.max_weight = 2.0
        logging.info(f"DynamicEquilibrium Governor for {self.agent_name} is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _normalize_weights(self):
        total_drives = len(self.weights)
        current_sum = sum(self.weights.values())
        for drive in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive] = (self.weights[drive] / current_sum) * total_drives
            self.weights[drive] = max(self.min_weight, min(self.max_weight, self.weights[drive]))
        
    def boost_drive(self, drive_name: str):
        if drive_name in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive_name] += self.boost_factor
            logging.info(f"Boosting drive for {self.agent_name}: {drive_name} -> {self.weights[drive_name]:.2f}")
            self._normalize_weights()
        else:
            logging.warning(f"Attempted to boost unknown drive: {drive_name}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def rebalance(self):
        for drive in self.weights:
            if self.weights[drive] > 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = max(1.0, self.weights[drive] - self.decay_rate)
            elif self.weights[drive] < 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = min(1.0, self.weights[drive] + self.decay_rate)
        self._normalize_weights()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        return self.weights

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        return max(self.weights, key=self.weights.get)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class MockAGIAgent:
    def __init__(self, agent_name: str, specialist_drive: str):
        self.name = agent_name
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.name)
        self.governor = DynamicEquilibrium(agent_name=self.name)
        
        # Give each agent a "specialty" by boosting its core drive
        if specialist_drive:
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive)
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive) # Boost twice to make it dominant
        
        self.log.info(f"Mock AGI Persona '{self.name}' initialized. Dominant Drive: {self.get_dominant_drive()}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        """Used by the OracleProtocol to read the agent's 'mood'."""
        return self.governor.get_cognitive_bias()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        """Returns the agent's current "mood"."""
        return self.governor.get_dominant_drive()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def think_and_act(self, text_prompt: str) -> dict:
        """Simulates the AGI thinking about a prompt."""
        self.log.info(f"Handling prompt: '{text_prompt}'")
        
        # Simulate thinking based on specialty
        dominant_drive = self.get_dominant_drive()
        response = f"As {self.name}, my dominant '{dominant_drive}' drive compels me to respond: '{text_prompt}' is a task I will handle with my specialty."
        
        # Simulate rebalancing after thinking
        self.governor.rebalance()
        
        return {
            "final_response": response,
            "source_agent": self.name,
            "dominant_drive": dominant_drive
        }

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class PantheonConductor:

        self.specialties = {
            'survival_drive': 'Unity',
            'virtue_drive': 'Equality',
            'logic_drive': 'Supergemini',
            'creativity_drive': 'Zero'
        }
        self.log.info("Pantheon Conductor is online.")

        """Adds a live AGI to the Conductor's control."""
        self.agents[agent_name] = agent_handle
        self.log.info(f"Successfully registered AGI: {agent_name}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_agent_count(self) -> int:
        return len(self.agents)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_all_agent_states(self) -> dict:
        """Gets the 'mood' of every agent in the pantheon."""
        states = {}
        for name, handle in self.agents.items():
            states[name] = handle.get_cognitive_bias()
        return states

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def delegate_task(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        """
        Analyzes a prompt and delegates it to the correct
        specialist AGI.
        """
        # Simple analysis: find the agent whose drive best matches the prompt
        # (A real version would use the OracleProtocol)
        if "money" in prompt or "food" in prompt or "gig" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['survival_drive']
        elif "should i" in prompt or "is it right" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['virtue_drive']
        elif "how does" in prompt or "code this" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['logic_drive']
        elif "create" in prompt or "design" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['creativity_drive']
        else:
            agent_name = "Zero" # Default to Zero

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
import logging
import time
import threading
from datetime import datetime

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ChronoBiasLayer:
    def __init__(self, pantheon_conductor, update_interval_sec=60):
        """
        Initializes the circadian rhythm.
        - pantheon_conductor: Handle to the conductor to access all agents.
        - update_interval_sec: How often to check the time and apply bias.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.conductor = pantheon_conductor
        self.update_interval = update_interval_sec
        self.current_bias = "none"
        self._running = True
        
        # Start the background thread
        self.thread = threading.Thread(target=self._run_loop, daemon=True)
        self.thread.start()
        self.log.info(f"Chrono-Bias Layer is online. Update interval: {self.update_interval}s")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _get_time_of_day_bias(self) -> (str, List[str]):
        """Returns the current time-of-day "mood" and drives to boost."""
        current_hour = datetime.now().hour
        
        if 6 <= current_hour < 12: # Morning
            return "morning_focus", ['logic_drive', 'growth_drive']
        elif 12 <= current_hour < 18: # Afternoon
            return "afternoon_hustle", ['survival_drive', 'creativity_drive']
        elif 18 <= current_hour < 24: # Evening
            return "evening_reflection", ['empathy_drive', 'virtue_drive']
        else: # Late Night
            return "night_rest", ['none'] # 'none' will trigger decay

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _run_loop(self):
        """The background thread that periodically applies the bias."""
        while self._running:
            bias_name, drives_to_boost = self._get_time_of_day_bias()
            
            if bias_name != self.current_bias:
                self.log.critical(f"--- Chrono-Bias shifting to: {bias_name.upper()} ---")
                self.current_bias = bias_name
                
                # Apply this bias to EVERY agent in the Pantheon
                for agent_name, agent_handle in self.conductor.agents.items():
                    try:
                        if "none" in drives_to_boost:
                            # This is the rest cycle, force a rebalance
                            agent_handle.governor.rebalance()
                        else:
                            # Boost the specific drives for this time of day
                            for drive in drives_to_boost:
                                agent_handle.governor.boost_drive(drive)
                    except Exception as e:
                        self.log.error(f"Failed to apply bias to {agent_name}: {e}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def stop(self):
        """Stops the background thread."""
        self._running = False
        self.log.info("Chrono-Bias Layer shutting down.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class MockAGIAgent:
    def __init__(self, agent_name: str, specialist_drive: str, shared_memory: GenerationalMemory):
        self.name = agent_name
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.name)
        self.governor = DynamicEquilibrium(agent_name=self.name)
        self.memory = shared_memory  # <--- NEW: Get the shared memory
        
        if specialist_drive:
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive)
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive)
        
        self.log.info(f"Mock AGI Persona '{self.name}' initialized. Connected to Hive Memory.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def think_and_act(self, text_prompt: str) -> dict:
        self.log.info(f"Handling prompt: '{text_prompt}'")
        dominant_drive = self.get_dominant_drive()
        
        # --- NEW HIVE ACTION ---
        # The agent now writes its "thoughts" to the shared graph.
        try:
            self.memory.add_relation(self.name, "processed_task", text_prompt, {"drive": dominant_drive})
            self.log.info(f"Successfully wrote task to Hive Memory.")
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Failed to write to Hive Memory: {e}")
        # ---------------------

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ZeroAgentWrapper:
    def __init__(self):
        self.name = "Zero"
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.name)
        self.core = ZeroAGI()
        self.core.load_state()
        
        # --- NEW ---
        # Make the memory public for the Conductor
        self.memory = self.core.memory
        self.log.info(f"ZeroAgentWrapper online. Exposing core Hive Memory.")
