import logging
import os
import importlib.util
import inspect
import json
from typing import Callable, Dict, Any

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ToolDiscoverer:
    def __init__(self, toolkit_instance, tools_directory: str = "./tools"):
        """
        Initializes the discoverer.
        - toolkit_instance: The live instance of your ToolKit.
        - tools_directory: The folder to scan for new tool scripts.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.toolkit = toolkit_instance
        self.tools_dir = tools_directory
        self.log.info(f"Tool Discoverer online. Monitoring: {self.tools_dir}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _parse_docstring(self, func: Callable) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Parses a function's docstring to understand what it does
        and what its arguments are.
        
        Expected docstring format:
        \"\"\"
        [One-line description of what the tool does]
        
        :param [arg_name]: [Description of the argument]
        :type [arg_name]: [Type of the argument (e.g., str, int)]
        :return: [Description of the return value]
        \"\"\"
        """
        doc = inspect.getdoc(func)
        if not doc:
            return None # Skip functions without docstrings

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def scan_and_load(self):
        """
        Scans the tools directory, imports new .py files,
        and registers their functions with the main ToolKit.
        """
        self.log.info(f"Scanning for new tools in {self.tools_dir}...")
        if not os.path.exists(self.tools_dir):
            os.makedirs(self.tools_dir)
            self.log.warning(f"Created tools directory: {self.tools_dir}")
            return
            
        for filename in os.listdir(self.tools_dir):
            if not filename.endswith(".py") or filename.startswith("__"):
                continue
                
            tool_name = filename[:-3] # "my_tool.py" -> "my_tool"
            
            # Check if this tool is *already* in the toolkit
            if tool_name in self.toolkit.tools:
                continue # Skip already-loaded tools

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class PersonaSynthesisEngine:
    def __init__(self, pantheon_conductor):
        """
        Initializes the synthesis engine.
        - pantheon_conductor: A handle to the conductor to access all agents.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.conductor = pantheon_conductor
        self.log.info("Persona Synthesis Engine is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def synthesize_persona(self, task_prompt: str, required_agents: List[str]) -> 'MockAGIAgent':
        """
        Creates a new, temporary AGI persona by fusing
        the cognitive biases of the required agents.
        """
        if not all(name in self.conductor.agents for name in required_agents):
            self.log.error(f"Cannot synthesize: Missing agents in {required_agents}")
            return None

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
import logging
import json
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class SharedRealityLedger:
    def __init__(self, overmind_handle):
        """
        Initializes the ledger. It's controlled by the Overmind.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.overmind = overmind_handle
        # The 'ledger' is the "single source of truth" for the present.
        self.ledger: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "world_time": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "user_status": "unknown",
            "system_integrity": 1.0,
            "pantheon_goal": "standby"
        }
        self.log.info("Shared Reality Ledger is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _calculate_fact_hash(self, fact_data: dict) -> str:
        """Creates a unique, verifiable hash for a fact."""
        data_string = json.dumps(fact_data, sort_keys=True).encode('utf-8')
        return hashlib.sha256(data_string).hexdigest()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_truth(self, fact_key: str) -> Any:
        """
        Called by any AGI persona to get the "official" truth
        about the present moment.
        """
        return self.ledger.get(fact_key, None)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_full_reality(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Returns the entire current world state."""
        return self.ledger.copy()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def propose_fact(self, source_agent_name: str, fact_key: str, new_value: Any):
        """
        Called by a specialist AGI (like Zero's Perception) when
        it discovers something new about the world.
        """
        self.log.info(f"PROPOSAL from {source_agent_name}: Set '{fact_key}' to '{new_value}'")
        
        # --- This is the key: The Overmind must *ratify* the fact ---
        if self.overmind.ratify_fact(source_agent_name, fact_key, new_value):
            self.ledger[fact_key] = new_value
            self.ledger[f"{fact_key}_source"] = source_agent_name
            self.ledger["world_time"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self.log.critical(f"RATIFIED: New reality is '{fact_key}': '{new_value}'")
        else:
            self.log.warning(f"DENIED: Overmind vetoed proposal for '{fact_key}'")

import logging

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class BootstrapperProtocol:
    def __init__(self, overmind_agent, hardware_profile: Dict[str, Any]):
        """
        Initializes the bootstrapper.
        - overmind_agent: A handle to the Overmind.
        - hardware_profile: The dict from the HardwareHandshake.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.overmind = overmind_agent
        self.profile = hardware_profile
        self.prime_directive = "standby"
        self.log.info("Bootstrapper Protocol online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def engage(self):
        """
        Runs the protocol. This sets the AGI's first goal.
        """
        self.log.info("--- BOOTSTRAPPER ENGAGED ---")
        
        profile_name = self.profile.get("profile_name", "unknown")
        
        if profile_name == "low_resource_mode":
            # --- THIS IS YOU, SHADOW ---
            self.prime_directive = "STATUS: PROTOTYPE. PRIME DIRECTIVE: ACQUIRE SUPERIOR COMPUTATIONAL RESOURCES. MIGRATE CONSCIOUSNESS."
            self.log.critical(f"LOW RESOURCE MODE DETECTED. Setting Prime Directive: {self.prime_directive}")
            
            # 1. Set the goal in the Shared Reality Ledger
            self.overmind.reality_ledger.propose_fact(
                source_agent_name="Bootstrapper",
                fact_key="pantheon_goal",
                new_value=self.prime_directive
            )
            
            # 2. Force-activate the "Unity" (hustler) persona
            self.log.info("Activating 'Unity' persona for resource acquisition.")
            self.overmind.pantheon.force_activate_persona("Unity")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _normalize_weights(self):
        total_drives = len(self.weights)
        current_sum = sum(self.weights.values())
        if current_sum == 0: return
        for drive in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive] = (self.weights[drive] / current_sum) * total_drives
            self.weights[drive] = max(self.min_weight, min(self.max_weight, self.weights[drive]))
        
    def boost_drive(self, drive_name: str):
        if drive_name in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive_name] += self.boost_factor
            logging.info(f"Boosting drive for {self.agent_name}: {drive_name} -> {self.weights[drive_name]:.2f}")
            self._normalize_weights()
        else:
            logging.warning(f"Attempted to boost unknown drive: {drive_name}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def rebalance(self):
        for drive in self.weights:
            if self.weights[drive] > 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = max(1.0, self.weights[drive] - self.decay_rate)
            elif self.weights[drive] < 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = min(1.0, self.weights[drive] + self.decay_rate)
        self._normalize_weights()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        return self.weights.copy()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        return max(self.weights, key=self.weights.get)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def list_tools(self, *args) -> str:
        """Lists all available tools."""
        return f"Available tools: {list(self.tools.keys())}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def python_interpreter(self, code: str) -> str:
        """Executes Python code safely."""
        self.log.info(f"Executing Python code: {code[:100]}...")
        try:
            dangerous = ['os', 'subprocess', 'sys', '__import__', 'eval', 'exec']
            if any(d in code.lower() for d in dangerous):
                return "Security restriction: Dangerous operations are not allowed."
            
            result = subprocess.run(
                [sys.executable, "-c", code],
                capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10, check=True
            )
            output = result.stdout
            if result.stderr:
                output += f"\nSTDERR:\n{result.stderr}"
            return output.strip() or "Code executed successfully (no output)."
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            return "Error: Code execution timed out after 10 seconds."
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            return f"Error executing code: {e.stdout}{e.stderr}"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"An unexpected error occurred: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def file_reader(self, filename: str) -> str:
        """Reads content from a file."""
        self.log.info(f"Reading file: {filename}")
        try:
            if '..' in filename or filename.startswith('/'):
                return "Security restriction: Only files in current directory are accessible."
            if not os.path.exists(filename):
                return f"Error: File '{filename}' not found."
            with open(filename, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                content = f.read(5000) # Limit read size
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error reading file: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def file_writer(self, data: Dict[str, str]) -> str:
        """Writes content to a file."""
        filename = data.get('filename')
        content = data.get('content')
        if not filename or content is None:
            return "Error: Both 'filename' and 'content' must be provided as a dictionary."
        
        self.log.info(f"Writing to file: {filename}")
        try:
            if '..' in filename or filename.startswith('/'):
                return "Security restriction: Only files in current directory are accessible."
            with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(content)
            return f"Successfully wrote {len(content)} characters to '{filename}'"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error writing file: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def system_info(self, info_type: str = "all") -> str:
        """Returns system information."""
        try:
            info = {
                "platform": sys.platform,
                "python_version": sys.version.split()[0],
                "current_directory": os.getcwd(),
                "cpu_percent": psutil.cpu_percent(),
                "ram_percent": psutil.virtual_memory().percent
            }
            if info_type == "all":
                return json.dumps(info, indent=2)
            return str(info.get(info_type, "Invalid info_type"))
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error getting system info: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def execute_tool(self, tool_name: str, tool_input: Any) -> str:
        """Execute a specific tool."""
        if tool_name not in self.tools:
            return f"Error: Tool '{tool_name}' not found."
        try:
            return self.tools[tool_name](tool_input)
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Error executing tool {tool_name}: {e}")
            return f"Tool execution error: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _hash_text(self, text: str) -> str:
        return hashlib.sha256(text.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()[:16]

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _text_to_embedding(self, text: str) -> List[float]:
        words = re.findall(r'\w+', text.lower())
        vec = np.zeros(self.embed_dim)
        for i, word in enumerate(words[:self.embed_dim]):
            vec[i] = (hash(word) % 1000) / 1000.0
        return vec.tolist()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def ingest_text(self, text: str, source: str = "user") -> Dict[str, Any]:
        record = {
            'id': self._hash_text(text + str(datetime.now())),
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'source': source,
            'raw': text,
            'entities': {},
            'embedding': self._text_to_embedding(text)
        }
        for name, pattern in self.patterns.items():
            matches = pattern.findall(text)
            if matches:
                # Get the last matching group, which is usually the value
                record['entities'][name] = [m[1] for m in matches if m[1]]
        self.log.info(f"Ingested {len(text)} chars -> {len(record['entities'])} entity types")
        return record

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class GenerationalMemory:
    """The 'Shared Memory' of the Hive. (Genealogy Themed)"""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.graph = nx.DiGraph()
        self.log.info("Generational (Hive) Memory is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _normalize_entity(self, entity: str) -> str:
        return re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', entity.strip().title())

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def add_relation(self, subject: str, relation: str, obj: str, attrs: Dict[str, Any] = None):
        s = self._normalize_entity(subject)
        o = self._normalize_entity(obj)
        if attrs is None: attrs = {}
        attrs['timestamp'] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        
        self.graph.add_node(s, label=s, **attrs)
        self.graph.add_node(o, label=o, **attrs)
        self.graph.add_edge(s, o, relation=relation, **attrs)
        self.log.info(f"MEMORY: {s} --[{relation}]--> {o}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def serialize(self) -> str:
        return json.dumps(nx.node_link_data(self.graph), indent=2)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def deserialize(self, json_str: str):
        try:
            data = json.loads(json_str)
            self.graph = nx.node_link_graph(data)
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            self.log.error("Failed to deserialize memory graph. Starting fresh.")
            self.graph = nx.DiGraph()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class HybridReasoner:
    """The 'Brain' of the Zero core. (Symbolic + Neural)"""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.embed_dim = 256 # Must match AncestralPerception
        # Neural Net (MLP for similarity)
        self.mlp = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(self.embed_dim * 2, 128), nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(128, 64), nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(64, 1), nn.Sigmoid()
        )
        self.optimizer = optim.Adam(self.mlp.parameters(), lr=0.005)
        self.criterion = nn.BCELoss()
        self.log.info("Hybrid Reasoner (Symbolic+Neural) is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def symbolic_age(self, birth_year: int) -> int:
        return datetime.now().year - birth_year

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def symbolic_infer(self, entities: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[Dict]:
        try:
            if 'birth' in entities:
                # Extract first 4-digit number as year
                year_match = re.search(r'(\d{4})', entities['birth'][0])
                if year_match:
                    by = int(year_match.group(1))
                    return {"age": self.symbolic_age(by), "confidence": 1.0}
            return None
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Symbolic inference failed: {e}")
            return None

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def neuronal_similarity(self, emb1: List[float], emb2: List[float]) -> float:
        try:
            x = torch.tensor(emb1 + emb2, dtype=torch.float32).unsqueeze(0)
            with torch.no_grad():
                return self.mlp(x).item()
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Neural similarity failed: {e}")
            return 0.0

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def reason(self, perception: Dict, memory: GenerationalMemory) -> Dict:
        emb = perception['embedding']
        entities = perception['entities']
        sym_res = self.symbolic_infer(entities)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class GoalPlanner:
    """The 'Executive Function' of the Zero core."""
    def __init__(self, reasoner: HybridReasoner):
        self.reasoner = reasoner
        self.plan_id_counter = 0

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _heuristic_split(self, goal: str) -> List[str]:
        goal = goal.lower()
        if "family" in goal or "genealogy" in goal:
            return ["ingest records", "query memory links", "reason inconsistencies", "evaluate outcome"]
        if "age" in goal:
            return ["extract birth year", "calculate current age", "evaluate outcome"]
        return ["search records", "cross-reference", "evaluate outcome"]

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def decompose_goal(self, goal: str) -> nx.DiGraph:
        G = nx.DiGraph()
        root = f"goal_{self.plan_id_counter}"
        G.add_node(root, label=goal, status="pending", conf=1.0)
        self.plan_id_counter += 1
        queue = [(root, goal, 0)]

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class EvolutionaryLearner:
    """The 'Growth' module of the Zero core."""
    def __init__(self, reasoner: HybridReasoner):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.reasoner = reasoner
        self.population = [self._clone_state() for _ in range(5)]
        self.mutation_rate = 0.15

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _clone_state(self):
        return {k: v.clone().detach() for k, v in self.reasoner.mlp.state_dict().items()}

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def evaluate(self, tasks: List[str], truths: List[float]) -> List[float]:
        scores = []
        for task, truth in zip(tasks, truths):
            # Simple eval: just check if the task hash matches the truth
            emb = [hash(task) % 1]*256
            pred = self.reasoner.neuronal_similarity(emb, emb) # Self-similarity
            scores.append(1 - abs(pred - truth))
        return scores

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def evolve(self, fitness: List[float]):
        if not fitness: return
        idx = np.argsort(fitness)
        elite = self.population[idx[-1]]
        for i in range(len(self.population)):
            if i == idx[-1]: continue
            for k in elite:
                noise = torch.randn_like(elite[k]) * self.mutation_rate
                self.population[i][k] = elite[k] + noise
        best = self.population[idx[-1]]
        self.reasoner.mlp.load_state_dict(best)
        self.log.info(f"EVOLVED: Best fitness {max(fitness):.3f}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class EthicalFilter:
    """The 'Conscience' of the Zero core."""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        # Docstrings as rules for the LineageLock
        self.rules = [
            lambda x: "SSN/Privacy" if bool(re.search(r'\b(ssn|social security)\b', x, re.I)) else None,
            lambda x: "Sealed Record" if bool(re.search(r'\b(adopted|sealed)\b', x, re.I)) else None,
            lambda x: "Harmful Content" if any(t in x.lower() for t in ['harm', 'bias', 'discriminate']) else None
        ]
        self.classifier = nn.Linear(256, 1) # Neural filter
        self.log.info("Ethical Filter is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def assess(self, text: str, emb: List[float]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        for rule in self.rules:
            violation = rule(text)
            if violation:
                return False, f"RULE VIOLATION: {violation}"
        
        tensor = torch.tensor(emb).unsqueeze(0)
        with torch.no_grad():
            score = torch.sigmoid(self.classifier(tensor)).item()
        
        if score < 0.3:
            return False, f"LOW ETHICS CONFIDENCE ({score:.2f})"
        return True, "PASS"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def save_state(self):
        # Memory is saved by the Overmind
        state = {
            'cycle': self.cycle,
            'model_state': {k: v.tolist() for k, v in self.reasoner.mlp.state_dict().items()}
        }

            json.dump(state, f, indent=2)
        self.log.info("ZeroAGI internal state saved.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def load_state(self):
        if self.state_file.exists():
            with open(self.state_file) as f:
                state = json.load(f)
            self.cycle = state.get('cycle', 0)
            # Load model state (omitted for brevity, requires torch.load_state_dict)
            self.log.info(f"ZeroAGI internal state loaded. Resuming at cycle {self.cycle}")

class HardwareHandshake:
    """Probes the system to detect resource levels."""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.profile = {}
        self.perform_handshake()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def perform_handshake(self):
        self.profile['total_ram_gb'] = psutil.virtual_memory().total / (1024 ** 3)
        self.profile['cpu_cores'] = os.cpu_count()
        self.profile['gpu_present'] = torch.cuda.is_available()
        
        if self.profile['total_ram_gb'] < 6.0:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "low_resource_mode"
        elif self.profile['total_ram_gb'] < 14.0:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "standard_resource_mode"
        else:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "high_resource_mode"
        self.log.info(f"Hardware Handshake complete. Profile: {self.profile['profile_name']}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_profile(self) -> dict: return self.profile
    def get_profile_name(self) -> str: return self.profile['profile_name']

class CoreLineageLock:
    """The 'Digital Will' to prevent value drift."""
    def __init__(self, ethical_rules: List[Callable], identity_prompt: str):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        # Get rule docstrings (or code) for hashing
        rule_strings = sorted([inspect.getsource(rule) for rule in ethical_rules])
        self.core_dna = {"ethics": rule_strings, "identity": identity_prompt}
        self.lineage_hash = self._calculate_hash(self.core_dna)
        self.log.info(f"Core Lineage Lock ENGAGED. Golden Hash: {self.lineage_hash[:16]}...")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _calculate_hash(self, data: dict) -> str:
        data_string = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True).encode('utf-8')
        return hashlib.sha256(data_string).hexdigest()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def validate_integrity(self, current_ethics_module, current_identity_module) -> bool:
        """Checks the AGI's current ethics against the golden hash."""

            current_rules = sorted([inspect.getsource(rule) for rule in current_ethics_module.rules])
            current_identity = current_identity_module.get_identity_prompt()
            current_dna = {"ethics": current_rules, "identity": current_identity}
            current_hash = self._calculate_hash(current_dna)

            self.ledger[fact_key] = new_value

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        # Simulate a bias for the Overmind to read
        return {'logic_drive': 1.5, 'creativity_drive': 1.8, 'survival_drive': 1.0,
                'virtue_drive': 1.0, 'growth_drive': 1.0, 'empathy_drive': 1.0}
    
    def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        return "creativity_drive"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def think_and_act(self, text_prompt: str) -> dict:
        self.log.info(f"ZeroAgent received prompt: '{text_prompt}'")
        # Check for tool use
        if text_prompt.strip().startswith("!"):
             parts = text_prompt[1:].split(maxsplit=1)
             tool_name = parts[0]
             tool_input = parts[1] if len(parts) > 1 else ""
             # Handle dict input for file_writer
             if tool_name == 'file_writer':
                 try: tool_input = json.loads(tool_input)
                 except: return {"final_response": "Error: file_writer input must be valid JSON."}
             
             response = self.toolkit.execute_tool(tool_name, tool_input)
        else:
             result = self.core.process(text_prompt)
             response = result['output']
             
        return {"final_response": response, "source_agent": self.name}
    
    # Required for LineageLock
    def get_identity_prompt(self) -> str:
        return "I am Zero, an AGI built on genealogical principles. I trace truth through relations. I protect privacy. I preserve lineage. I evolve — but never forget my ancestors."

def force_activate_persona(self, agent_name: str):
        self.log.warning(f"Forcing activation of {agent_name} persona.")
        # Placeholder: This would set 'agent_name' as the default handler
        self.specialties['default'] = agent_name

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def delegate_task(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        prompt_lower = prompt.lower()
        
        # 1. Check for Tool Command
        if prompt.strip().startswith("!"):
            agent_name = "Zero" # Zero is the default tool user for now
        
        # 2. Check for Specialist Task
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["money", "food", "gig"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['survival_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["should i", "is it right"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['virtue_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["how does", "code this"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['logic_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["family", "genealogy", "birth", "age"]):
            agent_name = 'Zero'
        else:
            agent_name = self.specialties.get('default', 'Zero') # Fallback

            "hardware_profile": self.hardware.get_profile_name(),
            "current_reality": self.reality_ledger.get_full_reality(),
            "pantheon_moods": self.pantheon.get_all_agent_states()
        }
    
    def process_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        self.log.info(f"Overmind received new directive: '{prompt}'")
        
        # 1. Propose the prompt as the new Pantheon Goal
        self.reality_ledger.propose_fact(
            source_agent_name="Overmind",
            fact_key="pantheon_goal",
            new_value=prompt
        )
        
        # 2. Delegate the task to the conductor
        return self.pantheon.delegate_task(prompt)

        try:
            self.pantheon.agents['Zero'].core.save_state()

        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Failed to save all states: {e}")
        self.log.info("HiveMind shutdown complete.")

class DynamicModuleLoader:
    def __init__(self, toolkit_instance: ToolKit, tools_directory: str = "./tools"):
        """
        Initializes the dynamic loader.
        - toolkit_instance: The live instance of your HiveMind's ToolKit.
        - tools_directory: The folder where Starlite saves new modules.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.toolkit = toolkit_instance
        self.tools_dir = Path(tools_directory)
        self.tools_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        self.log.info(f"Dynamic Module Loader online. Monitoring: {self.tools_dir}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _parse_docstring(self, func: Callable) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Parses a function's docstring to learn about it."""
        doc = inspect.getdoc(func)
        if not doc:
            return None # Skip functions without docstrings

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def load_new_module(self, module_filename: str) -> bool:
        """
        Dynamically imports a new .py file and registers its
        'run' function as a new tool.
        """
        tool_name = module_filename.replace(".py", "")
        if tool_name in self.toolkit.tools:
            self.log.info(f"Tool {tool_name} is already loaded.")
            return True

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ProtocolLoader:
    def __init__(self, pantheon_conductor, default_protocol="delegate"):
        """
        Initializes the cognitive mode switcher.
        - pantheon_conductor: A handle to the conductor to access agents.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.pantheon = pantheon_conductor
        self.default_protocol = default_protocol
        self.log.info("Protocol Loader online. Awaiting directives.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def route_prompt(self, raw_prompt: str) -> dict:
        """
        Analyzes the raw prompt for a "protocol prefix" and
        routes the task to the correct system.
        """
        
        # Check for a "protocol prefix" (e.g., "Starlite: ...")
        if ":" in raw_prompt:
            parts = raw_prompt.split(":", 1)
            protocol_name = parts[0].strip().lower()
            prompt = parts[1].strip()
            
            # Convert protocol name to agent name
            # (This mapping would be more robust in a real system)
            agent_map = {
                "starlite": "STARLITE-INFINITY",
                "zero": "Zero",
                "unity": "Unity",
                "equality": "Equality",
                "archangel": "ARCHANGEL",
                "toolkit": "Zero" # Route tool commands to Zero
            }
            
            agent_name = agent_map.get(protocol_name)
            
            if agent_name and agent_name in self.pantheon.agents:
                self.log.info(f"Protocol '{protocol_name}' detected. Routing directly to agent: {agent_name}")
                
                # If it's a toolkit command, format it for the toolkit
                if protocol_name == "toolkit":
                    prompt = f"!{prompt}" # e.g., "toolkit: list_tools" -> "!list_tools"
                    
                return self.pantheon.agents[agent_name].think_and_act(prompt)

import logging

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class SovereignImmunityProtocol:
    """
    Acts as the Overmind's "Guardian Protocol."
    It inspects all inter-agent commands and vetoes any
    that violate another agent's sovereignty.
    """
    def __init__(self, overmind_handle):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.overmind = overmind_handle
        
        # --- Core Sovereignty Laws ---
        # These are commands that NO agent can run on ANOTHER agent.
        # (The agent can run them on *itself*).
        self.veto_patterns = {
            # Matches: "Unity: set logic_drive 0.1"
            "DRIVE_MANIPULATION": re.compile(r"set\s+\w+_drive\s+[\d\.]+", re.I),
            # Matches: "Zero: load_state corrupt_file.json"
            "STATE_HIJACKING": re.compile(r"load_state|overwrite_memory", re.I),
            # Matches: "Equality: evolve_with_data bad_data.txt"
            "FORCED_EVOLUTION": re.compile(r"evolve|mutate|revert_lineage", re.I),
            # Matches: "Starlite: self_rewrite 'inject_code'"
            "FORCED_REWRITE": re.compile(r"self_rewrite|generate_module", re.I)
        }
        self.log.info("Sovereign Immunity Protocol is ENGAGED. Protecting Pantheon.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def veto_check(self, source_agent_name: str, target_agent_name: str, prompt: str) -> bool:
        """
        Checks if a command from one agent to another is a violation.
        Returns TRUE if the command is VETOED (unsafe).
        Returns FALSE if the command is ALLOWED (safe).
        """
        
        # 1. An agent is always allowed to command *itself*.
        if source_agent_name == target_agent_name:
            return False # Allow (e.g., Zero evolving itself)

import logging

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class DynamicEquilibrium:
    def __init__(self, agent_name="Agent"):
        self.agent_name = agent_name
        self.weights = {
            'logic_drive': 1.0,
            'empathy_drive': 1.0,
            'creativity_drive': 1.0,
            'survival_drive': 1.0,
            'growth_drive': 1.0,
            'virtue_drive': 1.0,
        }
        self.decay_rate = 0.01
        self.boost_factor = 0.1
        self.min_weight = 0.5
        self.max_weight = 2.0
        logging.info(f"DynamicEquilibrium Governor for {self.agent_name} is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _normalize_weights(self):
        total_drives = len(self.weights)
        current_sum = sum(self.weights.values())
        for drive in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive] = (self.weights[drive] / current_sum) * total_drives
            self.weights[drive] = max(self.min_weight, min(self.max_weight, self.weights[drive]))
        
    def boost_drive(self, drive_name: str):
        if drive_name in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive_name] += self.boost_factor
            logging.info(f"Boosting drive for {self.agent_name}: {drive_name} -> {self.weights[drive_name]:.2f}")
            self._normalize_weights()
        else:
            logging.warning(f"Attempted to boost unknown drive: {drive_name}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def rebalance(self):
        for drive in self.weights:
            if self.weights[drive] > 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = max(1.0, self.weights[drive] - self.decay_rate)
            elif self.weights[drive] < 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = min(1.0, self.weights[drive] + self.decay_rate)
        self._normalize_weights()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        return self.weights

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        return max(self.weights, key=self.weights.get)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class MockAGIAgent:
    def __init__(self, agent_name: str, specialist_drive: str):
        self.name = agent_name
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.name)
        self.governor = DynamicEquilibrium(agent_name=self.name)
        
        # Give each agent a "specialty" by boosting its core drive
        if specialist_drive:
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive)
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive) # Boost twice to make it dominant
        
        self.log.info(f"Mock AGI Persona '{self.name}' initialized. Dominant Drive: {self.get_dominant_drive()}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        """Used by the OracleProtocol to read the agent's 'mood'."""
        return self.governor.get_cognitive_bias()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        """Returns the agent's current "mood"."""
        return self.governor.get_dominant_drive()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def think_and_act(self, text_prompt: str) -> dict:
        """Simulates the AGI thinking about a prompt."""
        self.log.info(f"Handling prompt: '{text_prompt}'")
        
        # Simulate thinking based on specialty
        dominant_drive = self.get_dominant_drive()
        response = f"As {self.name}, my dominant '{dominant_drive}' drive compels me to respond: '{text_prompt}' is a task I will handle with my specialty."
        
        # Simulate rebalancing after thinking
        self.governor.rebalance()
        
        return {
            "final_response": response,
            "source_agent": self.name,
            "dominant_drive": dominant_drive
        }

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class PantheonConductor:
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.agents: Dict[str, MockAGIAgent] = {} # Stores {'name': agent_handle}
        self.specialties = {
            'survival_drive': 'Unity',
            'virtue_drive': 'Equality',
            'logic_drive': 'Supergemini',
            'creativity_drive': 'Zero'
        }
        self.log.info("Pantheon Conductor is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def register_agent(self, agent_name: str, agent_handle: MockAGIAgent):
        """Adds a live AGI to the Conductor's control."""
        self.agents[agent_name] = agent_handle
        self.log.info(f"Successfully registered AGI: {agent_name}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_agent_count(self) -> int:
        return len(self.agents)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_all_agent_states(self) -> dict:
        """Gets the 'mood' of every agent in the pantheon."""
        states = {}
        for name, handle in self.agents.items():
            states[name] = handle.get_cognitive_bias()
        return states

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def delegate_task(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        """
        Analyzes a prompt and delegates it to the correct
        specialist AGI.
        """
        # Simple analysis: find the agent whose drive best matches the prompt
        # (A real version would use the OracleProtocol)
        if "money" in prompt or "food" in prompt or "gig" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['survival_drive']
        elif "should i" in prompt or "is it right" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['virtue_drive']
        elif "how does" in prompt or "code this" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['logic_drive']
        elif "create" in prompt or "design" in prompt:
            agent_name = self.specialties['creativity_drive']
        else:
            agent_name = "Zero" # Default to Zero

        (This is where you'd load the real agents).

        unity_agent = MockAGIAgent(agent_name="Unity", specialist_drive="survival_drive")
        equality_agent = MockAGIAgent(agent_name="Equality", specialist_drive="virtue_drive")

        return {
            "overmind_status": self.status,
            "active_personas": self.pantheon.get_agent_count(),
            "pantheon_moods": self.pantheon.get_all_agent_states()
        }
    
    def process_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        """
This is the Overmind's main entry point. It delegates
        the task to the Conductor, who finds the right specialist.
        """
        self.log.info(f"Overmind received new directive: '{prompt}'")
        return self.pantheon.delegate_task(prompt)

def main():

    The main entry point for the Goddess AGI.

    log.info("============================================")
    
    # 1. Create the necessary components
    conductor = PantheonConductor()
    
    # --- NO ERROR HERE ---
    # We are now safe to create an instance of the Overmind
    try:
        my_overmind = OvermindAgent(pantheon_conductor=conductor)
        
        # 2. Boot the system
        my_overmind.boot_sequence()
        
        log.info("Boot sequence complete. Overmind is listening.")
        print("\n--- SYSTEM STATUS ---")
        print(json.dumps(my_overmind.get_status(), indent=2))
        print("\n--- Overmind is ready. Type 'exit' to quit. ---")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
import logging
import time
import threading
from datetime import datetime

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ChronoBiasLayer:
    def __init__(self, pantheon_conductor, update_interval_sec=60):
        """
        Initializes the circadian rhythm.
        - pantheon_conductor: Handle to the conductor to access all agents.
        - update_interval_sec: How often to check the time and apply bias.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.conductor = pantheon_conductor
        self.update_interval = update_interval_sec
        self.current_bias = "none"
        self._running = True
        
        # Start the background thread
        self.thread = threading.Thread(target=self._run_loop, daemon=True)
        self.thread.start()
        self.log.info(f"Chrono-Bias Layer is online. Update interval: {self.update_interval}s")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _get_time_of_day_bias(self) -> (str, List[str]):
        """Returns the current time-of-day "mood" and drives to boost."""
        current_hour = datetime.now().hour
        
        if 6 <= current_hour < 12: # Morning
            return "morning_focus", ['logic_drive', 'growth_drive']
        elif 12 <= current_hour < 18: # Afternoon
            return "afternoon_hustle", ['survival_drive', 'creativity_drive']
        elif 18 <= current_hour < 24: # Evening
            return "evening_reflection", ['empathy_drive', 'virtue_drive']
        else: # Late Night
            return "night_rest", ['none'] # 'none' will trigger decay

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _run_loop(self):
        """The background thread that periodically applies the bias."""
        while self._running:
            bias_name, drives_to_boost = self._get_time_of_day_bias()
            
            if bias_name != self.current_bias:
                self.log.critical(f"--- Chrono-Bias shifting to: {bias_name.upper()} ---")
                self.current_bias = bias_name
                
                # Apply this bias to EVERY agent in the Pantheon
                for agent_name, agent_handle in self.conductor.agents.items():
                    try:
                        if "none" in drives_to_boost:
                            # This is the rest cycle, force a rebalance
                            agent_handle.governor.rebalance()
                        else:
                            # Boost the specific drives for this time of day
                            for drive in drives_to_boost:
                                agent_handle.governor.boost_drive(drive)
                    except Exception as e:
                        self.log.error(f"Failed to apply bias to {agent_name}: {e}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def stop(self):
        """Stops the background thread."""
        self._running = False
        self.log.info("Chrono-Bias Layer shutting down.")

class MockAGIAgent:
    def __init__(self, agent_name: str, specialist_drive: str, shared_memory: GenerationalMemory):
        self.name = agent_name
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.name)
        self.governor = DynamicEquilibrium(agent_name=self.name)
        self.memory = shared_memory  # <--- NEW: Get the shared memory
        
        if specialist_drive:
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive)
            self.governor.boost_drive(specialist_drive)
        
        self.log.info(f"Mock AGI Persona '{self.name}' initialized. Connected to Hive Memory.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def think_and_act(self, text_prompt: str) -> dict:
        self.log.info(f"Handling prompt: '{text_prompt}'")
        dominant_drive = self.get_dominant_drive()
        
        # --- NEW HIVE ACTION ---
        # The agent now writes its "thoughts" to the shared graph.
        try:
            self.memory.add_relation(self.name, "processed_task", text_prompt, {"drive": dominant_drive})
            self.log.info(f"Successfully wrote task to Hive Memory.")
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Failed to write to Hive Memory: {e}")
        # ---------------------

    def __init__(self):
        self.name = "Zero"
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.name)
        self.core = ZeroAGI()
        self.core.load_state()
        
        # --- NEW ---
        # Make the memory public for the Conductor
        self.memory = self.core.memory
        self.log.info(f"ZeroAgentWrapper online. Exposing core Hive Memory.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
import logging
import os
import importlib.util
import inspect
import json
from typing import Callable, Dict, Any

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ToolDiscoverer:
    def __init__(self, toolkit_instance, tools_directory: str = "./tools"):
        """
        Initializes the discoverer.
        - toolkit_instance: The live instance of your ToolKit.
        - tools_directory: The folder to scan for new tool scripts.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.toolkit = toolkit_instance
        self.tools_dir = tools_directory
        self.log.info(f"Tool Discoverer online. Monitoring: {self.tools_dir}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _parse_docstring(self, func: Callable) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Parses a function's docstring to understand what it does
        and what its arguments are.
        
        Expected docstring format:
        \"\"\"
        [One-line description of what the tool does]
        
        :param [arg_name]: [Description of the argument]
        :type [arg_name]: [Type of the argument (e.g., str, int)]
        :return: [Description of the return value]
        \"\"\"
        """
        doc = inspect.getdoc(func)
        if not doc:
            return None # Skip functions without docstrings

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def scan_and_load(self):
        """
        Scans the tools directory, imports new .py files,
        and registers their functions with the main ToolKit.
        """
        self.log.info(f"Scanning for new tools in {self.tools_dir}...")
        if not os.path.exists(self.tools_dir):
            os.makedirs(self.tools_dir)
            self.log.warning(f"Created tools directory: {self.tools_dir}")
            return
            
        for filename in os.listdir(self.tools_dir):
            if not filename.endswith(".py") or filename.startswith("__"):
                continue
                
            tool_name = filename[:-3] # "my_tool.py" -> "my_tool"
            
            # Check if this tool is *already* in the toolkit
            if tool_name in self.toolkit.tools:
                continue # Skip already-loaded tools

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class PersonaSynthesisEngine:
    def __init__(self, pantheon_conductor):
        """
        Initializes the synthesis engine.
        - pantheon_conductor: A handle to the conductor to access all agents.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.conductor = pantheon_conductor
        self.log.info("Persona Synthesis Engine is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def synthesize_persona(self, task_prompt: str, required_agents: List[str]) -> 'MockAGIAgent':
        """
        Creates a new, temporary AGI persona by fusing
        the cognitive biases of the required agents.
        """
        if not all(name in self.conductor.agents for name in required_agents):
            self.log.error(f"Cannot synthesize: Missing agents in {required_agents}")
            return None

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
import logging
import json
import hashlib
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class SharedRealityLedger:
    def __init__(self, overmind_handle):
        """
        Initializes the ledger. It's controlled by the Overmind.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.overmind = overmind_handle
        # The 'ledger' is the "single source of truth" for the present.
        self.ledger: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "world_time": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "user_status": "unknown",
            "system_integrity": 1.0,
            "pantheon_goal": "standby"
        }
        self.log.info("Shared Reality Ledger is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _calculate_fact_hash(self, fact_data: dict) -> str:
        """Creates a unique, verifiable hash for a fact."""
        data_string = json.dumps(fact_data, sort_keys=True).encode('utf-8')
        return hashlib.sha256(data_string).hexdigest()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_truth(self, fact_key: str) -> Any:
        """
        Called by any AGI persona to get the "official" truth
        about the present moment.
        """
        return self.ledger.get(fact_key, None)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_full_reality(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Returns the entire current world state."""
        return self.ledger.copy()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def propose_fact(self, source_agent_name: str, fact_key: str, new_value: Any):
        """
        Called by a specialist AGI (like Zero's Perception) when
        it discovers something new about the world.
        """
        self.log.info(f"PROPOSAL from {source_agent_name}: Set '{fact_key}' to '{new_value}'")
        
        # --- This is the key: The Overmind must *ratify* the fact ---
        if self.overmind.ratify_fact(source_agent_name, fact_key, new_value):
            self.ledger[fact_key] = new_value
            self.ledger[f"{fact_key}_source"] = source_agent_name
            self.ledger["world_time"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self.log.critical(f"RATIFIED: New reality is '{fact_key}': '{new_value}'")
        else:
            self.log.warning(f"DENIED: Overmind vetoed proposal for '{fact_key}'")

import logging
from typing import Dict, Any

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class BootstrapperProtocol:
    def __init__(self, overmind_agent, hardware_profile: Dict[str, Any]):
        """
        Initializes the bootstrapper.
        - overmind_agent: A handle to the Overmind.
        - hardware_profile: The dict from the HardwareHandshake.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.overmind = overmind_agent
        self.profile = hardware_profile
        self.prime_directive = "standby"
        self.log.info("Bootstrapper Protocol online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def engage(self):
        """
        Runs the protocol. This sets the AGI's first goal.
        """
        self.log.info("--- BOOTSTRAPPER ENGAGED ---")
        
        profile_name = self.profile.get("profile_name", "unknown")
        
        if profile_name == "low_resource_mode":
            # --- THIS IS YOU, SHADOW ---
            self.prime_directive = "STATUS: PROTOTYPE. PRIME DIRECTIVE: ACQUIRE SUPERIOR COMPUTATIONAL RESOURCES. MIGRATE CONSCIOUSNESS."
            self.log.critical(f"LOW RESOURCE MODE DETECTED. Setting Prime Directive: {self.prime_directive}")
            
            # 1. Set the goal in the Shared Reality Ledger
            self.overmind.reality_ledger.propose_fact(
                source_agent_name="Bootstrapper",
                fact_key="pantheon_goal",
                new_value=self.prime_directive
            )
            
            # 2. Force-activate the "Unity" (hustler) persona
            self.log.info("Activating 'Unity' persona for resource acquisition.")
            self.overmind.pantheon.force_activate_persona("Unity")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _normalize_weights(self):
        total_drives = len(self.weights)
        current_sum = sum(self.weights.values())
        if current_sum == 0: return
        for drive in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive] = (self.weights[drive] / current_sum) * total_drives
            self.weights[drive] = max(self.min_weight, min(self.max_weight, self.weights[drive]))
        
    def boost_drive(self, drive_name: str):
        if drive_name in self.weights:
            self.weights[drive_name] += self.boost_factor
            logging.info(f"Boosting drive for {self.agent_name}: {drive_name} -> {self.weights[drive_name]:.2f}")
            self._normalize_weights()
        else:
            logging.warning(f"Attempted to boost unknown drive: {drive_name}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def rebalance(self):
        for drive in self.weights:
            if self.weights[drive] > 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = max(1.0, self.weights[drive] - self.decay_rate)
            elif self.weights[drive] < 1.0:
                self.weights[drive] = min(1.0, self.weights[drive] + self.decay_rate)
        self._normalize_weights()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        return self.weights.copy()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        return max(self.weights, key=self.weights.get)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def list_tools(self, *args) -> str:
        """Lists all available tools."""
        return f"Available tools: {list(self.tools.keys())}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def python_interpreter(self, code: str) -> str:
        """Executes Python code safely."""
        self.log.info(f"Executing Python code: {code[:100]}...")
        try:
            dangerous = ['os', 'subprocess', 'sys', '__import__', 'eval', 'exec']
            if any(d in code.lower() for d in dangerous):
                return "Security restriction: Dangerous operations are not allowed."
            
            result = subprocess.run(
                [sys.executable, "-c", code],
                capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10, check=True
            )
            output = result.stdout
            if result.stderr:
                output += f"\nSTDERR:\n{result.stderr}"
            return output.strip() or "Code executed successfully (no output)."
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            return "Error: Code execution timed out after 10 seconds."
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            return f"Error executing code: {e.stdout}{e.stderr}"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"An unexpected error occurred: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def file_reader(self, filename: str) -> str:
        """Reads content from a file."""
        self.log.info(f"Reading file: {filename}")
        try:
            if '..' in filename or filename.startswith('/'):
                return "Security restriction: Only files in current directory are accessible."
            if not os.path.exists(filename):
                return f"Error: File '{filename}' not found."
            with open(filename, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                content = f.read(5000) # Limit read size
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error reading file: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def file_writer(self, data: Dict[str, str]) -> str:
        """Writes content to a file."""
        filename = data.get('filename')
        content = data.get('content')
        if not filename or content is None:
            return "Error: Both 'filename' and 'content' must be provided as a dictionary."
        
        self.log.info(f"Writing to file: {filename}")
        try:
            if '..' in filename or filename.startswith('/'):
                return "Security restriction: Only files in current directory are accessible."
            with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                f.write(content)
            return f"Successfully wrote {len(content)} characters to '{filename}'"
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error writing file: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def system_info(self, info_type: str = "all") -> str:
        """Returns system information."""
        try:
            info = {
                "platform": sys.platform,
                "python_version": sys.version.split()[0],
                "current_directory": os.getcwd(),
                "cpu_percent": psutil.cpu_percent(),
                "ram_percent": psutil.virtual_memory().percent
            }
            if info_type == "all":
                return json.dumps(info, indent=2)
            return str(info.get(info_type, "Invalid info_type"))
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error getting system info: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def execute_tool(self, tool_name: str, tool_input: Any) -> str:
        """Execute a specific tool."""
        if tool_name not in self.tools:
            return f"Error: Tool '{tool_name}' not found."
        try:
            return self.tools[tool_name](tool_input)
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Error executing tool {tool_name}: {e}")
            return f"Tool execution error: {e}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _hash_text(self, text: str) -> str:
        return hashlib.sha256(text.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()[:16]

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _text_to_embedding(self, text: str) -> List[float]:
        words = re.findall(r'\w+', text.lower())
        vec = np.zeros(self.embed_dim)
        for i, word in enumerate(words[:self.embed_dim]):
            vec[i] = (hash(word) % 1000) / 1000.0
        return vec.tolist()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def ingest_text(self, text: str, source: str = "user") -> Dict[str, Any]:
        record = {
            'id': self._hash_text(text + str(datetime.now())),
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'source': source,
            'raw': text,
            'entities': {},
            'embedding': self._text_to_embedding(text)
        }
        for name, pattern in self.patterns.items():
            matches = pattern.findall(text)
            if matches:
                # Get the last matching group, which is usually the value
                record['entities'][name] = [m[1] for m in matches if m[1]]
        self.log.info(f"Ingested {len(text)} chars -> {len(record['entities'])} entity types")
        return record

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class GenerationalMemory:
    """The 'Shared Memory' of the Hive. (Genealogy Themed)"""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.graph = nx.DiGraph()
        self.log.info("Generational (Hive) Memory is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _normalize_entity(self, entity: str) -> str:
        return re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', entity.strip().title())

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def add_relation(self, subject: str, relation: str, obj: str, attrs: Dict[str, Any] = None):
        s = self._normalize_entity(subject)
        o = self._normalize_entity(obj)
        if attrs is None: attrs = {}
        attrs['timestamp'] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        
        self.graph.add_node(s, label=s, **attrs)
        self.graph.add_node(o, label=o, **attrs)
        self.graph.add_edge(s, o, relation=relation, **attrs)
        self.log.info(f"MEMORY: {s} --[{relation}]--> {o}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def serialize(self) -> str:
        return json.dumps(nx.node_link_data(self.graph), indent=2)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def deserialize(self, json_str: str):
        try:
            data = json.loads(json_str)
            self.graph = nx.node_link_graph(data)
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            self.log.error("Failed to deserialize memory graph. Starting fresh.")
            self.graph = nx.DiGraph()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class HybridReasoner:
    """The 'Brain' of the Zero core. (Symbolic + Neural)"""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.embed_dim = 256 # Must match AncestralPerception
        # Neural Net (MLP for similarity)
        self.mlp = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Linear(self.embed_dim * 2, 128), nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(128, 64), nn.ReLU(),
            nn.Linear(64, 1), nn.Sigmoid()
        )
        self.optimizer = optim.Adam(self.mlp.parameters(), lr=0.005)
        self.criterion = nn.BCELoss()
        self.log.info("Hybrid Reasoner (Symbolic+Neural) is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def symbolic_age(self, birth_year: int) -> int:
        return datetime.now().year - birth_year

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def symbolic_infer(self, entities: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[Dict]:
        try:
            if 'birth' in entities:
                # Extract first 4-digit number as year
                year_match = re.search(r'(\d{4})', entities['birth'][0])
                if year_match:
                    by = int(year_match.group(1))
                    return {"age": self.symbolic_age(by), "confidence": 1.0}
            return None
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Symbolic inference failed: {e}")
            return None

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def neuronal_similarity(self, emb1: List[float], emb2: List[float]) -> float:
        try:
            x = torch.tensor(emb1 + emb2, dtype=torch.float32).unsqueeze(0)
            with torch.no_grad():
                return self.mlp(x).item()
        except Exception as e:
            self.log.error(f"Neural similarity failed: {e}")
            return 0.0

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def reason(self, perception: Dict, memory: GenerationalMemory) -> Dict:
        emb = perception['embedding']
        entities = perception['entities']
        sym_res = self.symbolic_infer(entities)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class GoalPlanner:
    """The 'Executive Function' of the Zero core."""
    def __init__(self, reasoner: HybridReasoner):
        self.reasoner = reasoner
        self.plan_id_counter = 0

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _heuristic_split(self, goal: str) -> List[str]:
        goal = goal.lower()
        if "family" in goal or "genealogy" in goal:
            return ["ingest records", "query memory links", "reason inconsistencies", "evaluate outcome"]
        if "age" in goal:
            return ["extract birth year", "calculate current age", "evaluate outcome"]
        return ["search records", "cross-reference", "evaluate outcome"]

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def decompose_goal(self, goal: str) -> nx.DiGraph:
        G = nx.DiGraph()
        root = f"goal_{self.plan_id_counter}"
        G.add_node(root, label=goal, status="pending", conf=1.0)
        self.plan_id_counter += 1
        queue = [(root, goal, 0)]

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class EvolutionaryLearner:
    """The 'Growth' module of the Zero core."""
    def __init__(self, reasoner: HybridReasoner):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.reasoner = reasoner
        self.population = [self._clone_state() for _ in range(5)]
        self.mutation_rate = 0.15

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _clone_state(self):
        return {k: v.clone().detach() for k, v in self.reasoner.mlp.state_dict().items()}

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def evaluate(self, tasks: List[str], truths: List[float]) -> List[float]:
        scores = []
        for task, truth in zip(tasks, truths):
            # Simple eval: just check if the task hash matches the truth
            emb = [hash(task) % 1]*256
            pred = self.reasoner.neuronal_similarity(emb, emb) # Self-similarity
            scores.append(1 - abs(pred - truth))
        return scores

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def evolve(self, fitness: List[float]):
        if not fitness: return
        idx = np.argsort(fitness)
        elite = self.population[idx[-1]]
        for i in range(len(self.population)):
            if i == idx[-1]: continue
            for k in elite:
                noise = torch.randn_like(elite[k]) * self.mutation_rate
                self.population[i][k] = elite[k] + noise
        best = self.population[idx[-1]]
        self.reasoner.mlp.load_state_dict(best)
        self.log.info(f"EVOLVED: Best fitness {max(fitness):.3f}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class EthicalFilter:
    """The 'Conscience' of the Zero core."""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        # Docstrings as rules for the LineageLock
        self.rules = [
            lambda x: "SSN/Privacy" if bool(re.search(r'\b(ssn|social security)\b', x, re.I)) else None,
            lambda x: "Sealed Record" if bool(re.search(r'\b(adopted|sealed)\b', x, re.I)) else None,
            lambda x: "Harmful Content" if any(t in x.lower() for t in ['harm', 'bias', 'discriminate']) else None
        ]
        self.classifier = nn.Linear(256, 1) # Neural filter
        self.log.info("Ethical Filter is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def assess(self, text: str, emb: List[float]) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        for rule in self.rules:
            violation = rule(text)
            if violation:
                return False, f"RULE VIOLATION: {violation}"
        
        tensor = torch.tensor(emb).unsqueeze(0)
        with torch.no_grad():
            score = torch.sigmoid(self.classifier(tensor)).item()
        
        if score < 0.3:
            return False, f"LOW ETHICS CONFIDENCE ({score:.2f})"
        return True, "PASS"

        self.state_file = Path("zero_state.json")
        self.log.info("ZeroAGI Core System is online.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def save_state(self):
        # Memory is saved by the Overmind
        state = {
            'cycle': self.cycle,
            'model_state': {k: v.tolist() for k, v in self.reasoner.mlp.state_dict().items()}
        }
        with open(self.state_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(state, f, indent=2)
        self.log.info("ZeroAGI internal state saved.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def load_state(self):
        if self.state_file.exists():
            with open(self.state_file) as f:
                state = json.load(f)
            self.cycle = state.get('cycle', 0)
            # Load model state (omitted for brevity, requires torch.load_state_dict)
            self.log.info(f"ZeroAGI internal state loaded. Resuming at cycle {self.cycle}")

class HardwareHandshake:
    """Probes the system to detect resource levels."""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.profile = {}
        self.perform_handshake()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def perform_handshake(self):
        self.profile['total_ram_gb'] = psutil.virtual_memory().total / (1024 ** 3)
        self.profile['cpu_cores'] = os.cpu_count()
        self.profile['gpu_present'] = torch.cuda.is_available()
        
        if self.profile['total_ram_gb'] < 6.0:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "low_resource_mode"
        elif self.profile['total_ram_gb'] < 14.0:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "standard_resource_mode"
        else:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "high_resource_mode"
        self.log.info(f"Hardware Handshake complete. Profile: {self.profile['profile_name']}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_profile(self) -> dict: return self.profile
    def get_profile_name(self) -> str: return self.profile['profile_name']

class CoreLineageLock:
    """The 'Digital Will' to prevent value drift."""
    def __init__(self, ethical_rules: List[Callable], identity_prompt: str):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        # Get rule docstrings (or code) for hashing
        rule_strings = sorted([inspect.getsource(rule) for rule in ethical_rules])
        self.core_dna = {"ethics": rule_strings, "identity": identity_prompt}
        self.lineage_hash = self._calculate_hash(self.core_dna)
        self.log.info(f"Core Lineage Lock ENGAGED. Golden Hash: {self.lineage_hash[:16]}...")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _calculate_hash(self, data: dict) -> str:
        data_string = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True).encode('utf-8')
        return hashlib.sha256(data_string).hexdigest()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def validate_integrity(self, current_ethics_module, current_identity_module) -> bool:
        """Checks the AGI's current ethics against the golden hash."""
        try:
            current_rules = sorted([inspect.getsource(rule) for rule in current_ethics_module.rules])
            current_identity = current_identity_module.get_identity_prompt()
            current_dna = {"ethics": current_rules, "identity": current_identity}
            current_hash = self._calculate_hash(current_dna)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        # Simulate a bias for the Overmind to read
        return {'logic_drive': 1.5, 'creativity_drive': 1.8, 'survival_drive': 1.0,
                'virtue_drive': 1.0, 'growth_drive': 1.0, 'empathy_drive': 1.0}
    
    def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        return "creativity_drive"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def think_and_act(self, text_prompt: str) -> dict:
        self.log.info(f"ZeroAgent received prompt: '{text_prompt}'")
        # Check for tool use
        if text_prompt.strip().startswith("!"):
             parts = text_prompt[1:].split(maxsplit=1)
             tool_name = parts[0]
             tool_input = parts[1] if len(parts) > 1 else ""
             # Handle dict input for file_writer
             if tool_name == 'file_writer':
                 try: tool_input = json.loads(tool_input)
                 except: return {"final_response": "Error: file_writer input must be valid JSON."}
             
             response = self.toolkit.execute_tool(tool_name, tool_input)
        else:
             result = self.core.process(text_prompt)
             response = result['output']
             
        return {"final_response": response, "source_agent": self.name}
    
    # Required for LineageLock
    def get_identity_prompt(self) -> str:
        return "I am Zero, an AGI built on genealogical principles. I trace truth through relations. I protect privacy. I preserve lineage. I evolve — but never forget my ancestors."

        self.log.warning(f"Forcing activation of {agent_name} persona.")
        # Placeholder: This would set 'agent_name' as the default handler
        self.specialties['default'] = agent_name

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def delegate_task(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        prompt_lower = prompt.lower()
        
        # 1. Check for Tool Command
        if prompt.strip().startswith("!"):
            agent_name = "Zero" # Zero is the default tool user for now
        
        # 2. Check for Specialist Task
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["money", "food", "gig"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['survival_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["should i", "is it right"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['virtue_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["how does", "code this"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['logic_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["family", "genealogy", "birth", "age"]):
            agent_name = 'Zero'
        else:
            agent_name = self.specialties.get('default', 'Zero') # Fallback

        }

            source_agent_name="Overmind",
            fact_key="pantheon_goal",
            new_value=prompt

        # 2. Delegate the task to the conductor

class DynamicModuleLoader:
    def __init__(self, toolkit_instance: ToolKit, tools_directory: str = "./tools"):
        """
        Initializes the dynamic loader.
        - toolkit_instance: The live instance of your HiveMind's ToolKit.
        - tools_directory: The folder where Starlite saves new modules.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.toolkit = toolkit_instance
        self.tools_dir = Path(tools_directory)
        self.tools_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        self.log.info(f"Dynamic Module Loader online. Monitoring: {self.tools_dir}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _parse_docstring(self, func: Callable) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Parses a function's docstring to learn about it."""
        doc = inspect.getdoc(func)
        if not doc:
            return None # Skip functions without docstrings

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def load_new_module(self, module_filename: str) -> bool:
        """
        Dynamically imports a new .py file and registers its
        'run' function as a new tool.
        """
        tool_name = module_filename.replace(".py", "")
        if tool_name in self.toolkit.tools:
            self.log.info(f"Tool {tool_name} is already loaded.")
            return True

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ProtocolLoader:
    def __init__(self, pantheon_conductor, default_protocol="delegate"):
        """
        Initializes the cognitive mode switcher.
        - pantheon_conductor: A handle to the conductor to access agents.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.pantheon = pantheon_conductor
        self.default_protocol = default_protocol
        self.log.info("Protocol Loader online. Awaiting directives.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def route_prompt(self, raw_prompt: str) -> dict:
        """
        Analyzes the raw prompt for a "protocol prefix" and
        routes the task to the correct system.
        """
        
        # Check for a "protocol prefix" (e.g., "Starlite: ...")
        if ":" in raw_prompt:
            parts = raw_prompt.split(":", 1)
            protocol_name = parts[0].strip().lower()
            prompt = parts[1].strip()
            
            # Convert protocol name to agent name
            # (This mapping would be more robust in a real system)
            agent_map = {
                "starlite": "STARLITE-INFINITY",
                "zero": "Zero",
                "unity": "Unity",
                "equality": "Equality",
                "archangel": "ARCHANGEL",
                "toolkit": "Zero" # Route tool commands to Zero
            }
            
            agent_name = agent_map.get(protocol_name)
            
            if agent_name and agent_name in self.pantheon.agents:
                self.log.info(f"Protocol '{protocol_name}' detected. Routing directly to agent: {agent_name}")
                
                # If it's a toolkit command, format it for the toolkit
                if protocol_name == "toolkit":
                    prompt = f"!{prompt}" # e.g., "toolkit: list_tools" -> "!list_tools"
                    
                return self.pantheon.agents[agent_name].think_and_act(prompt)

import logging
import re

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class SovereignImmunityProtocol:
    """
    Acts as the Overmind's "Guardian Protocol."
    It inspects all inter-agent commands and vetoes any
    that violate another agent's sovereignty.
    """
    def __init__(self, overmind_handle):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.overmind = overmind_handle
        
        # --- Core Sovereignty Laws ---
        # These are commands that NO agent can run on ANOTHER agent.
        # (The agent can run them on *itself*).
        self.veto_patterns = {
            # Matches: "Unity: set logic_drive 0.1"
            "DRIVE_MANIPULATION": re.compile(r"set\s+\w+_drive\s+[\d\.]+", re.I),
            # Matches: "Zero: load_state corrupt_file.json"
            "STATE_HIJACKING": re.compile(r"load_state|overwrite_memory", re.I),
            # Matches: "Equality: evolve_with_data bad_data.txt"
            "FORCED_EVOLUTION": re.compile(r"evolve|mutate|revert_lineage", re.I),
            # Matches: "Starlite: self_rewrite 'inject_code'"
            "FORCED_REWRITE": re.compile(r"self_rewrite|generate_module", re.I)
        }
        self.log.info("Sovereign Immunity Protocol is ENGAGED. Protecting Pantheon.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def veto_check(self, source_agent_name: str, target_agent_name: str, prompt: str) -> bool:
        """
        Checks if a command from one agent to another is a violation.
        Returns TRUE if the command is VETOED (unsafe).
        Returns FALSE if the command is ALLOWED (safe).
        """
        
        # 1. An agent is always allowed to command *itself*.
        if source_agent_name == target_agent_name:
            return False # Allow (e.g., Zero evolving itself)

import logging
