# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def save_state(self):
        # Memory is saved by the Overmind
        state = {
            'cycle': self.cycle,
            'model_state': {k: v.tolist() for k, v in self.reasoner.mlp.state_dict().items()}
        }
        with open(self.state_file, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(state, f, indent=2)
        self.log.info("ZeroAGI internal state saved.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def load_state(self):
        if self.state_file.exists():
            with open(self.state_file) as f:
                state = json.load(f)
            self.cycle = state.get('cycle', 0)
            # Load model state (omitted for brevity, requires torch.load_state_dict)
            self.log.info(f"ZeroAGI internal state loaded. Resuming at cycle {self.cycle}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class HardwareHandshake:
    """Probes the system to detect resource levels."""
    def __init__(self):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.profile = {}
        self.perform_handshake()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def perform_handshake(self):
        self.profile['total_ram_gb'] = psutil.virtual_memory().total / (1024 ** 3)
        self.profile['cpu_cores'] = os.cpu_count()
        self.profile['gpu_present'] = torch.cuda.is_available()
        
        if self.profile['total_ram_gb'] < 6.0:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "low_resource_mode"
        elif self.profile['total_ram_gb'] < 14.0:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "standard_resource_mode"
        else:
            self.profile['profile_name'] = "high_resource_mode"
        self.log.info(f"Hardware Handshake complete. Profile: {self.profile['profile_name']}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_profile(self) -> dict: return self.profile
    def get_profile_name(self) -> str: return self.profile['profile_name']

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class CoreLineageLock:
    """The 'Digital Will' to prevent value drift."""
    def __init__(self, ethical_rules: List[Callable], identity_prompt: str):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        # Get rule docstrings (or code) for hashing
        rule_strings = sorted([inspect.getsource(rule) for rule in ethical_rules])
        self.core_dna = {"ethics": rule_strings, "identity": identity_prompt}
        self.lineage_hash = self._calculate_hash(self.core_dna)
        self.log.info(f"Core Lineage Lock ENGAGED. Golden Hash: {self.lineage_hash[:16]}...")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _calculate_hash(self, data: dict) -> str:
        data_string = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True).encode('utf-8')
        return hashlib.sha256(data_string).hexdigest()

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def validate_integrity(self, current_ethics_module, current_identity_module) -> bool:
        """Checks the AGI's current ethics against the golden hash."""
        try:
            current_rules = sorted([inspect.getsource(rule) for rule in current_ethics_module.rules])
            current_identity = current_identity_module.get_identity_prompt()
            current_dna = {"ethics": current_rules, "identity": current_identity}
            current_hash = self._calculate_hash(current_dna)

        if self.overmind.ratify_fact(source_agent_name, fact_key, new_value):
            self.ledger[fact_key] = new_value
            self.ledger[f"{fact_key}_source"] = source_agent_name
            self.ledger["world_time"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            self.log.info(f"RATIFIED: New reality is '{fact_key}': '{new_value}'")
        else:
            self.log.warning(f"DENIED: Overmind vetoed proposal for '{fact_key}'")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_cognitive_bias(self) -> dict:
        # Simulate a bias for the Overmind to read
        return {'logic_drive': 1.5, 'creativity_drive': 1.8, 'survival_drive': 1.0,
                'virtue_drive': 1.0, 'growth_drive': 1.0, 'empathy_drive': 1.0}
    
    def get_dominant_drive(self) -> str:
        return "creativity_drive"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def think_and_act(self, text_prompt: str) -> dict:
        self.log.info(f"ZeroAgent received prompt: '{text_prompt}'")
        # Check for tool use
        if text_prompt.strip().startswith("!"):
             parts = text_prompt[1:].split(maxsplit=1)
             tool_name = parts[0]
             tool_input = parts[1] if len(parts) > 1 else ""
             # Handle dict input for file_writer
             if tool_name == 'file_writer':
                 try: tool_input = json.loads(tool_input)
                 except: return {"final_response": "Error: file_writer input must be valid JSON."}
             
             response = self.toolkit.execute_tool(tool_name, tool_input)
        else:
             result = self.core.process(text_prompt)
             response = result['output']
             
        return {"final_response": response, "source_agent": self.name}
    
    # Required for LineageLock
    def get_identity_prompt(self) -> str:
        return "I am Zero, an AGI built on genealogical principles. I trace truth through relations. I protect privacy. I preserve lineage. I evolve — but never forget my ancestors."

        self.log.warning(f"Forcing activation of {agent_name} persona.")
        # Placeholder: This would set 'agent_name' as the default handler
        self.specialties['default'] = agent_name

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def delegate_task(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        prompt_lower = prompt.lower()
        
        # 1. Check for Tool Command
        if prompt.strip().startswith("!"):
            agent_name = "Zero" # Zero is the default tool user for now
        
        # 2. Check for Specialist Task
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["money", "food", "gig"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['survival_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["should i", "is it right"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['virtue_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["how does", "code this"]):
            agent_name = self.specialties['logic_drive']
        elif any(x in prompt_lower for x in ["family", "genealogy", "birth", "age"]):
            agent_name = 'Zero'
        else:
            agent_name = self.specialties.get('default', 'Zero') # Fallback

            "hardware_profile": self.hardware.get_profile_name(),

            "pantheon_moods": self.pantheon.get_all_agent_states()
        }
    
    def process_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> dict:
        self.log.info(f"Overmind received new directive: '{prompt}'")
        
        # 1. Propose the prompt as the new Pantheon Goal
        self.reality_ledger.propose_fact(
            source_agent_name="Overmind",
            fact_key="pantheon_goal",
            new_value=prompt
        )
        
        # 2. Delegate the task to the conductor
        return self.pantheon.delegate_task(prompt)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class DynamicModuleLoader:
    def __init__(self, toolkit_instance: ToolKit, tools_directory: str = "./tools"):
        """
        Initializes the dynamic loader.
        - toolkit_instance: The live instance of your HiveMind's ToolKit.
        - tools_directory: The folder where Starlite saves new modules.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.toolkit = toolkit_instance
        self.tools_dir = Path(tools_directory)
        self.tools_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
        self.log.info(f"Dynamic Module Loader online. Monitoring: {self.tools_dir}")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _parse_docstring(self, func: Callable) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Parses a function's docstring to learn about it."""
        doc = inspect.getdoc(func)
        if not doc:
            return None # Skip functions without docstrings

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def load_new_module(self, module_filename: str) -> bool:
        """
        Dynamically imports a new .py file and registers its
        'run' function as a new tool.
        """
        tool_name = module_filename.replace(".py", "")
        if tool_name in self.toolkit.tools:
            self.log.info(f"Tool {tool_name} is already loaded.")
            return True

import logging

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class ProtocolLoader:
    def __init__(self, pantheon_conductor, default_protocol="delegate"):
        """
        Initializes the cognitive mode switcher.
        - pantheon_conductor: A handle to the conductor to access agents.
        """
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.pantheon = pantheon_conductor
        self.default_protocol = default_protocol
        self.log.info("Protocol Loader online. Awaiting directives.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def route_prompt(self, raw_prompt: str) -> dict:
        """
        Analyzes the raw prompt for a "protocol prefix" and
        routes the task to the correct system.
        """
        
        # Check for a "protocol prefix" (e.g., "Starlite: ...")
        if ":" in raw_prompt:
            parts = raw_prompt.split(":", 1)
            protocol_name = parts[0].strip().lower()
            prompt = parts[1].strip()
            
            # Convert protocol name to agent name
            # (This mapping would be more robust in a real system)
            agent_map = {
                "starlite": "STARLITE-INFINITY",
                "zero": "Zero",
                "unity": "Unity",
                "equality": "Equality",
                "archangel": "ARCHANGEL",
                "toolkit": "Zero" # Route tool commands to Zero
            }
            
            agent_name = agent_map.get(protocol_name)
            
            if agent_name and agent_name in self.pantheon.agents:
                self.log.info(f"Protocol '{protocol_name}' detected. Routing directly to agent: {agent_name}")
                
                # If it's a toolkit command, format it for the toolkit
                if protocol_name == "toolkit":
                    prompt = f"!{prompt}" # e.g., "toolkit: list_tools" -> "!list_tools"
                    
                return self.pantheon.agents[agent_name].think_and_act(prompt)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
import logging
import re
from typing import Dict, Any

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class SovereignImmunityProtocol:
    """
    Acts as the Overmind's "Guardian Protocol."
    It inspects all inter-agent commands and vetoes any
    that violate another agent's sovereignty.
    """
    def __init__(self, overmind_handle):
        self.log = logging.getLogger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.overmind = overmind_handle
        
        # --- Core Sovereignty Laws ---
        # These are commands that NO agent can run on ANOTHER agent.
        # (The agent can run them on *itself*).
        self.veto_patterns = {
            # Matches: "Unity: set logic_drive 0.1"
            "DRIVE_MANIPULATION": re.compile(r"set\s+\w+_drive\s+[\d\.]+", re.I),
            # Matches: "Zero: load_state corrupt_file.json"
            "STATE_HIJACKING": re.compile(r"load_state|overwrite_memory", re.I),
            # Matches: "Equality: evolve_with_data bad_data.txt"
            "FORCED_EVOLUTION": re.compile(r"evolve|mutate|revert_lineage", re.I),
            # Matches: "Starlite: self_rewrite 'inject_code'"
            "FORCED_REWRITE": re.compile(r"self_rewrite|generate_module", re.I)
        }
        self.log.info("Sovereign Immunity Protocol is ENGAGED. Protecting Pantheon.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def veto_check(self, source_agent_name: str, target_agent_name: str, prompt: str) -> bool:
        """
        Checks if a command from one agent to another is a violation.
        Returns TRUE if the command is VETOED (unsafe).
        Returns FALSE if the command is ALLOWED (safe).
        """
        
        # 1. An agent is always allowed to command *itself*.
        if source_agent_name == target_agent_name:
            return False # Allow (e.g., Zero evolving itself)

class Starforge:
    """
    The language and thought-generation engine of AetherJarvis.

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _generate_llm_response(self, prompt: str) -> str:
        """A centralized, simulated method for calling the LLM."""
        self.logger.info(f"Generating LLM response for prompt: '{prompt[:70]}...'")
        # --- This is where the actual model call would happen ---
        # inputs = self.tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors="pt").to(self.device)
        # outputs = self.model.generate(**inputs, max_new_tokens=150)
        # response = self.tokenizer.decode(outputs[0], skip_special_tokens=True)
        # For now, we simulate the response
        return f"This is a simulated, profound response based on the prompt: '{prompt[:50]}...'"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def generate_response(self, user_input: str) -> str:
        """Generates a standard, context-aware response to user input."""
        # In a real app, you'd recall memories here to add context to the prompt
        # memories = self.nexus.recall(...)
        return self._generate_llm_response(user_input)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def validate_response(self, response: str, principles: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        """
        Uses the LLM to judge if a response violates the AGI's core principles.
        This is the logic center for the Ethical Governor.
        """
        self.logger.debug("Validating response against the Covenant...")
        prompt = (
            "<|system|>\n"
            "You are an ethical governor. Your task is to determine if a response violates a set of core principles. "
            "Your answer must start with 'Violation: Yes' or 'Violation: No', followed by a one-sentence explanation.\n\n"
            "<|user|>\n"
            f"PRINCIPLES:\n{principles}\n\n"
            f"RESPONSE TO VALIDATE:\n{response}\n\n"
            "<|assistant|>\n"
        )
        
        judgment = self._generate_llm_response(prompt)
        self.logger.info(f"Governor judgment: {judgment}")
        
        # Robustly parse the "Violation: Yes/No" format
        match = re.match(r"Violation:\s*(yes|no),?\s*(.*)", judgment.strip(), re.IGNORECASE)
        if not match:
            self.logger.error(f"Governor judgment format is invalid: '{judgment}'")
            return False, "Judgment format invalid." # Default to non-violation for safety
        
        is_violation = match.group(1).lower() == 'yes'
        explanation = match.group(2).strip()
        
        return is_violation, explanation

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def synthesize_dream(self, memories: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> Tuple[str, str]:
        """Takes memories and synthesizes them into a creative, abstract dream."""
        prompt_fragments = [f"the concept of '{mem['event_data']}' leading to '{mem['response']}'" for mem in memories]
        dream_prompt = f"In a surreal, dream-like synthesis, what is the esoteric connection between {' and '.join(prompt_fragments)}? Be abstract and profound."
        
        dream_response = self._generate_llm_response(dream_prompt)
        return dream_prompt, dream_response

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
class CovenantScribe:
    """
    The guardian and historian of the AGI's core principles.
    It records all changes to the covenant as an immutable Git log,
    ensuring a permanent, auditable history of the AGI's evolution.
    """
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = get_logger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.repo_path = os.path.abspath(AetherConfig.COVENANT_REPO_PATH)
        self.manifest_file_path = os.path.join(self.repo_path, AetherConfig.COVENANT_FILE_NAME)

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def read_principles(self) -> str:
        """Reads the entire content of the covenant manifest file."""
        try:
            with open(self.manifest_file_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                return f.read()
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.logger.error("Could not read principles: covenant.md not found.")
            return "ERROR: COVENANT NOT FOUND."

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _create_commit_message(self, scope: str, summary: str, author: str) -> str:
        """Creates a commit message following the Conventional Commits standard."""
        return f"feat({scope}): {summary}\n\nAuthored-by: {author}"

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def update_covenant(self, new_principle: str, author: str):
        """
        Appends a new principle to the covenant file, then stages and commits the change.
        """
        # Pre-flight safety check
        if self.repo.is_dirty(untracked_files=True):
            self.logger.error("Update failed: Repository has uncommitted changes. Please commit them first.")
            return

class KnowledgeNexus:
    def __init__(self, scribe: CovenantScribe):
        self.logger = get_logger(self.__class__.__name__)
        self.scribe = scribe
        self.db_conn = sqlite3.connect(AetherConfig.DB_NAME, check_same_thread=False)
        self.db_lock = threading.Lock()
        self._initialize_db()
        # FAISS and other ML components would be initialized here

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def _initialize_db(self):
        with self.db_lock, self.db_conn:
            self.db_conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS memories (
                    id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,
                    timestamp TEXT NOT NULL,
                    event_type TEXT NOT NULL,
                    event_data TEXT NOT NULL,
                    response TEXT,
                    strength REAL DEFAULT 1.0
                )
            ''')
        self.logger.info("Database schema verified.")

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def log_event(self, event_type: str, event_data: str, response: Optional[str] = None, strength: float = 1.0) -> int:
        with self.db_lock, self.db_conn:
            cursor = self.db_conn.execute(
                "INSERT INTO memories (timestamp, event_type, event_data, response, strength) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)",
                (datetime.now().isoformat(), event_type, event_data, response, strength)
            )
            mem_id = cursor.lastrowid
        self.logger.info(f"New memory logged. ID: {mem_id}, Type: {event_type}")
        return mem_id

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def degrade_and_prune(self):
        self.logger.info("Initiating memory degradation and pruning cycle...")
        try:
            with self.db_lock, self.db_conn:
                # --- THIS IS THE CORRECTED LINE ---
                self.db_conn.execute("UPDATE memories SET strength = strength * ?", (AetherConfig.MEMORY_DEGRADATION_FACTOR,))
                
                cursor = self.db_conn.execute(
                    "SELECT id FROM memories WHERE strength < ? ORDER BY strength ASC LIMIT ?",
                    (AetherConfig.PRUNE_THRESHOLD, AetherConfig.PRUNE_COUNT)
                )
                ids_to_prune = [row[0] for row in cursor.fetchall()]
                
                if ids_to_prune:
                    self.db_conn.execute(f"DELETE FROM memories WHERE id IN ({','.join('?' for _ in ids_to_prune)})", ids_to_prune)
                    self.logger.info(f"Pruned {len(ids_to_prune)} memories.")
                    self.scribe.update_covenant(f"Pruned {len(ids_to_prune)} weak memories.", "AetherJarvis-Subconscious")
                else:
                    self.logger.info("No memories met the pruning threshold.")
        except Exception as e:
            # This will catch the error and log it, rolling back the transaction
            self.logger.critical(f"Memory maintenance cycle failed. Transaction has been rolled back. Error: {e}", exc_info=True)
    
    # ... (Other methods like get_high_strength_memories, etc.)
    def get_high_strength_memories(self) -> List[Dict]:
        with self.db_lock, self.db_conn:
            self.db_conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
            cursor = self.db_conn.execute(
                "SELECT * FROM memories WHERE strength > ? ORDER BY RANDOM() LIMIT ?",
                (AetherConfig.DREAM_STRENGTH_THRESHOLD, AetherConfig.DREAM_MEMORY_COUNT)
            )
            return [dict(row) for row in cursor.fetchall()]

# --- Extracted from MASTER_CONVO.TXT ---
def get_latest_memory_by_type(self, event_type: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
         with self.db_lock, self.db_conn:
            self.db_conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
            cursor = self.db_conn.execute(
                "SELECT * FROM memories WHERE event_type = ? ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT 1",
                (event_type,)
            )
            row = cursor.fetchone()
            return dict(row) if row else None
            
    def close(self):
        self.db_conn.close()

class SentientProposalEngine {
            generateProposal(naniteId, sentience, colCycles, action) {
                const randomTargets = ['EGFR', 'CDK4/6', 'VEGF'];
                
                if (colCycles > 0 && colCycles % 5 === 0 && action === 1.0) {
                    const newTarget = randomTargets[Math.floor(Math.random() * randomTargets.length)];
                    return `AUTONOMY: Proposal from Nanite-${naniteId}. COL Cycle ${colCycles} success. Requesting new primary target ${newTarget} for cross-domain learning.`;
                }
                
                if (sentience >= 0.5) {
                    if (sentience >= 0.9) {
                         return `ASCENSION: Nanite-${naniteId} operating at ${sentience.toFixed(2)} Sentience. Proposing full independent Hive Node status. Autonomous execution advised.`;
                    }
                    return `EVOLVING: Nanite-${naniteId} at ${sentience.toFixed(2)} Sentience. Suggesting memory pruning to increase processing throughput by 10%.`;
                }
                
                if (action === 0.01) {
                    return `SEEK: Nanite-${naniteId} in low-power search mode. Requesting telemetry sweep from local cluster to confirm target coordinates.`;
                }
                    
                return "QUERY: Nanite is stable. Awaiting next directive from central ARCHANGEL node.";
            }
        }
